# <a name="host-aspnet-core-on-windows-with-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-103">在使用 IIS 的 Windows 上裝載 ASP.NET Core</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-103">Host ASP.NET Core on Windows with IIS</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-104">如需將 ASP.NET Core 應用程式發佈至 IIS 伺服器的教學課程體驗，請參閱<xref:tutorials/publish-to-iis>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-104">For a tutorial experience on publishing an ASP.NET Core app to an IIS server, see <xref:tutorials/publish-to-iis>.</span></span>

[<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-105">安裝 .NET Core 裝載套件組合</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-105">Install the .NET Core Hosting Bundle</span></span>](#install-the-net-core-hosting-bundle)

## <a name="supported-operating-systems"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-106">支援的作業系統</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-106">Supported operating systems</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-107">以下為支援的作業系統：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-107">The following operating systems are supported:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-108">Windows 7 或更新版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-108">Windows 7 or later</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-109">Windows Server 2012 R2 或更新版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-109">Windows Server 2012 R2 or later</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-110">[HTTP.sys 伺服器](xref:fundamentals/servers/httpsys) (先前稱為 WebListener) 不適用搭配 IIS 的反向 Proxy 設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-110">[HTTP.sys server](xref:fundamentals/servers/httpsys) (formerly called WebListener) doesn't work in a reverse proxy configuration with IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-111">請使用 [Kestrel 伺服器](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-111">Use the [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-112">如需在 Azure 中裝載的資訊，請參閱 <xref:host-and-deploy/azure-apps/index>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-112">For information on hosting in Azure, see <xref:host-and-deploy/azure-apps/index>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-113">如需疑難排解指引，請參閱 <xref:test/troubleshoot>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-113">For troubleshooting guidance, see <xref:test/troubleshoot>.</span></span>

## <a name="supported-platforms"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-114">支援的平台</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-114">Supported platforms</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-115">支援針對 32 位元 (x86) 或 64 位元 (x64) 部署發行的應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-115">Apps published for 32-bit (x86) or 64-bit (x64) deployment are supported.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-116">使用 32 位元 (x86) .NET Core SDK 部署 32 位元應用程式，除非應用程式：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-116">Deploy a 32-bit app with a 32-bit (x86) .NET Core SDK unless the app:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-117">需要提供給 64 位元應用程式使用的較大虛擬記憶體位址空間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-117">Requires the larger virtual memory address space available to a 64-bit app.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-118">需要較大的 IIS 堆疊大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-118">Requires the larger IIS stack size.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-119">有 64 位元原生相依性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-119">Has 64-bit native dependencies.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-120">針對32位 (x86) 發佈的應用程式必須為其 IIS 應用程式集區啟用32位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-120">Apps published for 32-bit (x86) must have 32-bit enabled for their IIS Application Pools.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-121">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[建立 IIS 網站](#create-the-iis-site)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-121">For more information, see the [Create the IIS site](#create-the-iis-site) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-122">使用 64 位元 (x64) .NET Core SDK 來發行 64 位元應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-122">Use a 64-bit (x64) .NET Core SDK to publish a 64-bit app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-123">主機系統上必須有 64 位元執行階段存在。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-123">A 64-bit runtime must be present on the host system.</span></span>

## <a name="hosting-models"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-124">裝載模型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-124">Hosting models</span></span>

### <a name="in-process-hosting-model"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-125">同處理序裝載模型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-125">In-process hosting model</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-126">使用同處理序裝載，ASP.NET Core 應用程式會在與其 IIS 工作者處理序相同的處理序中執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-126">Using in-process hosting, an ASP.NET Core app runs in the same process as its IIS worker process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-127">因為要求未透過回送介面卡 (將連出網路流量傳回同一部電腦的網路介面) 進行 proxy 處理，所以同處理序裝載會提供優於跨處理序裝載的效能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-127">In-process hosting provides improved performance over out-of-process hosting because requests aren't proxied over the loopback adapter, a network interface that returns outgoing network traffic back to the same machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-128">IIS 透過 [Windows 處理序啟用服務 (WAS)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was) 來執行處理程序管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-128">IIS handles process management with the [Windows Process Activation Service (WAS)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-129">[ASP.NET Core 模組](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module)：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-129">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module):</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-130">執行應用程式初始化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-130">Performs app initialization.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-131">載入 [CoreCLR](/dotnet/standard/glossary#coreclr)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-131">Loads the [CoreCLR](/dotnet/standard/glossary#coreclr).</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-132">呼叫 `Program.Main`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-132">Calls `Program.Main`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-133">處理 IIS 原生要求的存留期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-133">Handles the lifetime of the IIS native request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-134">下圖說明 IIS、ASP.NET Core 模組和同處理序裝載應用程式之間的關聯性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-134">The following diagram illustrates the relationship between IIS, the ASP.NET Core Module, and an app hosted in-process:</span></span>

![同處理序代管內的 ASP.NET Core 模組案例](index/_static/ancm-inprocess.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-136">要求會從 Web 到達核心模式的 HTTP.sys 驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-136">A request arrives from the web to the kernel-mode HTTP.sys driver.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-137">驅動程式會在網站設定的連接埠上將原生要求路由至 IIS，此連接埠通常是 80 (HTTP) 或 443 (HTTPS)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-137">The driver routes the native request to IIS on the website's configured port, usually 80 (HTTP) or 443 (HTTPS).</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-138">ASP.NET Core 模組會接收原生要求，並將它傳遞給 IIS HTTP 伺服器 (`IISHttpServer`) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-138">The ASP.NET Core Module receives the native request and passes it to IIS HTTP Server (`IISHttpServer`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-139">IIS HTTP 伺服器是 IIS 的同處理序伺服程式實作，可將要求從原生轉換為受控。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-139">IIS HTTP Server is an in-process server implementation for IIS that converts the request from native to managed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-140">在 IIS HTTP 伺服器處理要求之後：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-140">After the IIS HTTP Server processes the request:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-141">要求會傳送至 ASP.NET Core 中介軟體管線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-141">The request is sent to the ASP.NET Core middleware pipeline.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-142">中介軟體管線會處理要求，並將其作為 `HttpContext` 執行個體傳遞至應用程式的邏輯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-142">The middleware pipeline handles the request and passes it on as an `HttpContext` instance to the app's logic.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-143">應用程式的回應會透過 IIS HTTP 伺服器傳回 IIS。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-143">The app's response is passed back to IIS through IIS HTTP Server.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-144">IIS 會將回應傳送到起始該要求的用戶端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-144">IIS sends the response to the client that initiated the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-145">同進程裝載是加入宣告現有的應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-145">In-process hosting is opt-in for existing apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-146">ASP.NET Core 的 web 範本會使用同進程裝載模型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-146">The ASP.NET Core web templates use the in-process hosting model.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-147">`CreateDefaultBuilder` 會透過呼叫 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIIS*> 方法來啟動 [CoreCLR](/dotnet/standard/glossary#coreclr) 以新增 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.Server.IServer>，並在 IIS 工作者處理序 (*w3wp.exe* 或 *iisexpress.exe*) 內裝載應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-147">`CreateDefaultBuilder` adds an <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.Server.IServer> instance by calling the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIIS*> method to boot the [CoreCLR](/dotnet/standard/glossary#coreclr) and host the app inside of the IIS worker process (*w3wp.exe* or *iisexpress.exe*).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-148">效能測試指出，相較於將 .NET Core 應用程式裝載於處理序外，並將要求 Proxy 處理至 [Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel)，裝載於處理序內可提供明顯更高的要求輸送量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-148">Performance tests indicate that hosting a .NET Core app in-process delivers significantly higher request throughput compared to hosting the app out-of-process and proxying requests to [Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-149">發佈為單一檔案可執行檔的應用程式無法由同處理序裝載模型載入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-149">Apps published as a single file executable can't be loaded by the in-process hosting model.</span></span>

### <a name="out-of-process-hosting-model"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-150">跨處理序裝載模型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-150">Out-of-process hosting model</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-151">因為 ASP.NET Core 應用程式會在與 IIS 背景工作進程不同的進程中執行，所以 ASP.NET Core 模組會處理進程管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-151">Because ASP.NET Core apps run in a process separate from the IIS worker process, the ASP.NET Core Module handles process management.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-152">此模組會在第一個要求到達時啟動 ASP.NET Core 應用程式的處理序，並在應用程式關閉或損毀時將它重新啟動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-152">The module starts the process for the ASP.NET Core app when the first request arrives and restarts the app if it shuts down or crashes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-153">此行為基本上與執行同處理序，並由 [Windows 處理序啟用服務 (WAS)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was) 所管理的應用程式相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-153">This is essentially the same behavior as seen with apps that run in-process that are managed by the [Windows Process Activation Service (WAS)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-154">下圖說明 IIS、ASP.NET Core 模組和跨處理序裝載應用程式之間的關聯性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-154">The following diagram illustrates the relationship between IIS, the ASP.NET Core Module, and an app hosted out-of-process:</span></span>

![非同處理序代管內的 ASP.NET Core 模組案例](index/_static/ancm-outofprocess.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-156">要求會從 Web 到達核心模式的 HTTP.sys 驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-156">Requests arrive from the web to the kernel-mode HTTP.sys driver.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-157">驅動程式會將要求路由至網站設定之埠上的 IIS。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-157">The driver routes the requests to IIS on the website's configured port.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-158">設定的埠通常是 80 (HTTP) 或 443 (HTTPS) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-158">The configured port is usually 80 (HTTP) or 443 (HTTPS).</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-159">模組會在應用程式的隨機埠上將要求轉送至 Kestrel。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-159">The module forwards the requests to Kestrel on a random port for the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-160">隨機埠不是80或443。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-160">The random port isn't 80 or 443.</span></span>

<!-- make this a bullet list -->
<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-161">ASP.NET Core 模組會在啟動時透過環境變數指定埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-161">The ASP.NET Core Module specifies the port via an environment variable at startup.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-162">延伸模組會設定 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIISIntegration*> 伺服器來接聽 `http://localhost:{PORT}` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-162">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIISIntegration*> extension configures the server to listen on `http://localhost:{PORT}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-163">將會執行額外檢查，不是源自模組的要求都會遭到拒絕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-163">Additional checks are performed, and requests that don't originate from the module are rejected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-164">模組不支援 HTTPS 轉送。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-164">The module doesn't support HTTPS forwarding.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-165">即使 IIS 透過 HTTPS 接收，要求還是會透過 HTTP 轉送。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-165">Requests are forwarded over HTTP even if received by IIS over HTTPS.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-166">在 Kestrel 拾取來自模組的要求之後，會將要求轉送至 ASP.NET Core 中介軟體管線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-166">After Kestrel picks up the request from the module, the request is forwarded into the ASP.NET Core middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-167">中介軟體管線會處理要求，並將其作為 `HttpContext` 執行個體傳遞至應用程式的邏輯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-167">The middleware pipeline handles the request and passes it on as an `HttpContext` instance to the app's logic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-168">IIS Integration 新增的中介軟體會更新配置、遠端 IP 和帳戶路徑基底，以將要求轉送至 Kestrel。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-168">Middleware added by IIS Integration updates the scheme, remote IP, and pathbase to account for forwarding the request to Kestrel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-169">應用程式的回應會傳回 IIS，將它轉送回起始要求的 HTTP 用戶端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-169">The app's response is passed back to IIS, which forwards it back to the HTTP client that initiated the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-170">如需 ASP.NET Core 模組組態指南，請參閱 <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-170">For ASP.NET Core Module configuration guidance, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-171">如需代管的詳細資訊，請參閱[在 ASP.NET Core 中代管](xref:fundamentals/index#host)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-171">For more information on hosting, see [Host in ASP.NET Core](xref:fundamentals/index#host).</span></span>

## <a name="application-configuration"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-172">應用程式設定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-172">Application configuration</span></span>

### <a name="enable-the-iisintegration-components"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-173">啟用 IISIntegration 元件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-173">Enable the IISIntegration components</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-174">在 `CreateHostBuilder` (*Program.cs*) 中建立主機時，請呼叫 <xref:Microsoft.Extensions.Hosting.Host.CreateDefaultBuilder*> 以啟用 IIS 整合：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-174">When building a host in `CreateHostBuilder` (*Program.cs*), call <xref:Microsoft.Extensions.Hosting.Host.CreateDefaultBuilder*> to enable IIS integration:</span></span>

```csharp
public static IHostBuilder CreateHostBuilder(string[] args) =>
    Host.CreateDefaultBuilder(args)
        ...
```

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-175">如需 `CreateDefaultBuilder` 的詳細資訊，請參閱 <xref:fundamentals/host/generic-host#default-builder-settings>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-175">For more information on `CreateDefaultBuilder`, see <xref:fundamentals/host/generic-host#default-builder-settings>.</span></span>

### <a name="iis-options"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-176">IIS 選項</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-176">IIS options</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-177">**同處理序主控模型**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-177">**In-process hosting model**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-178">若要設定 IIS 伺服器選項，請在 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*> 中加入 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISServerOptions> 的服務設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-178">To configure IIS Server options, include a service configuration for <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISServerOptions> in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-179">下列範例會停用 AutomaticAuthentication：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-179">The following example disables AutomaticAuthentication:</span></span>

```csharp
services.Configure<IISServerOptions>(options => 
{
    options.AutomaticAuthentication = false;
});
```

| <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-180">選項</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-180">Option</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-181">預設</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-181">Default</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-182">設定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-182">Setting</span></span> |
| ------------------------------ | :-----: | ------- |
| `AutomaticAuthentication`      | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-183">若為 `true`，IIS 伺服器會設定由 [Windows 驗證](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth)所驗證的 `HttpContext.User`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-183">If `true`, IIS Server sets the `HttpContext.User` authenticated by [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-184">若為 `false`，則伺服器僅會對 `HttpContext.User` 提供身分識別，並在 `AuthenticationScheme` 明確要求時回應挑戰。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-184">If `false`, the server only provides an identity for `HttpContext.User` and responds to challenges when explicitly requested by the `AuthenticationScheme`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-185">必須在 IIS 中啟用 Windows 驗證以讓 `AutomaticAuthentication` 作用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-185">Windows Authentication must be enabled in IIS for `AutomaticAuthentication` to function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-186">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [Windows 驗證](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-186">For more information, see [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> |
| `AuthenticationDisplayName`    | `null`  | <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-187">設定使用者在登入頁面上看到的顯示名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-187">Sets the display name shown to users on login pages.</span></span> |
| `AllowSynchronousIO`           | `false` | <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-188">是否允許和的同步 i/o `HttpContext.Request` `HttpContext.Response` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-188">Whether synchronous I/O is allowed for the `HttpContext.Request` and the `HttpContext.Response`.</span></span> |
| `MaxRequestBodySize`           | `30000000`  | <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-189">取得或設定 `HttpRequest` 的要求本文大小上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-189">Gets or sets the max request body size for the `HttpRequest`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-190">請注意，IIS 本身具有限制 `maxAllowedContentLength`，此限制將在 `IISServerOptions` 中設定 `MaxRequestBodySize` 時處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-190">Note that IIS itself has the limit `maxAllowedContentLength` which will be processed before the `MaxRequestBodySize` set in the `IISServerOptions`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-191">變更 `MaxRequestBodySize` 將不會影響 `maxAllowedContentLength`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-191">Changing the `MaxRequestBodySize` won't affect the `maxAllowedContentLength`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-192">若要增加 `maxAllowedContentLength`，請在 *web.config* 中新增項目，以將 `maxAllowedContentLength` 設定為較高的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-192">To increase `maxAllowedContentLength`, add an entry in the *web.config* to set `maxAllowedContentLength` to a higher value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-193">如需更多詳細資料，請參閱[組態](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/requestFiltering/requestLimits/#configuration)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-193">For more details, see [Configuration](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/requestFiltering/requestLimits/#configuration).</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-194">**跨處理序裝載模型**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-194">**Out-of-process hosting model**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-195">若要設定 IIS 選項，請在 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*> 中加入 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISOptions> 的服務設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-195">To configure IIS options, include a service configuration for <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISOptions> in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-196">下列範例會防止應用程式填入 `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate`：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-196">The following example prevents the app from populating `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.Configure<IISOptions>(options => 
{
    options.ForwardClientCertificate = false;
});
```

| <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-197">選項</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-197">Option</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-198">預設</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-198">Default</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-199">設定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-199">Setting</span></span> |
| ------------------------------ | :-----: | ------- |
| `AutomaticAuthentication`      | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-200">若為 `true`，[IIS 整合中介軟體](#enable-the-iisintegration-components)會設定由 [Windows 驗證](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth)所驗證的 `HttpContext.User`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-200">If `true`, [IIS Integration Middleware](#enable-the-iisintegration-components) sets the `HttpContext.User` authenticated by [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-201">如果為 `false`，則驗證中介軟體僅針對 `HttpContext.User` 提供身分識別，並在游 `AuthenticationScheme` 提出明確要求時回應挑戰。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-201">If `false`, the middleware only provides an identity for `HttpContext.User` and responds to challenges when explicitly requested by the `AuthenticationScheme`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-202">必須在 IIS 中啟用 Windows 驗證以讓 `AutomaticAuthentication` 作用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-202">Windows Authentication must be enabled in IIS for `AutomaticAuthentication` to function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-203">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [Windows 驗證](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth)主題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-203">For more information, see the [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth) topic.</span></span> |
| `AuthenticationDisplayName`    | `null`  | <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-204">設定使用者在登入頁面上看到的顯示名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-204">Sets the display name shown to users on login pages.</span></span> |
| `ForwardClientCertificate`     | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-205">如果為 `true` 且 `MS-ASPNETCORE-CLIENTCERT` 要求標頭已存在，則會填入 `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-205">If `true` and the `MS-ASPNETCORE-CLIENTCERT` request header is present, the `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate` is populated.</span></span> |

### <a name="proxy-server-and-load-balancer-scenarios"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-206">Proxy 伺服器和負載平衡器案例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-206">Proxy server and load balancer scenarios</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-207">[IIS 整合中介軟體](#enable-the-iisintegration-components)和 ASP.NET Core 模組已設定為轉送：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-207">The [IIS Integration Middleware](#enable-the-iisintegration-components) and the ASP.NET Core Module are configured to forward the:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-208">配置 (HTTP/HTTPS) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-208">Scheme (HTTP/HTTPS).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-209">發出要求的遠端 IP 位址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-209">Remote IP address where the request originated.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-210">[IIS 整合中介軟體](#enable-the-iisintegration-components)會設定轉送的標頭中介軟體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-210">The [IIS Integration Middleware](#enable-the-iisintegration-components) configures Forwarded Headers Middleware.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-211">其他 Proxy 伺服器和負載平衡器後方託管的應用程式可能需要其他設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-211">Additional configuration might be required for apps hosted behind additional proxy servers and load balancers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-212">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[設定 ASP.NET Core 以處理 Proxy 伺服器和負載平衡器](xref:host-and-deploy/proxy-load-balancer)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-212">For more information, see [Configure ASP.NET Core to work with proxy servers and load balancers](xref:host-and-deploy/proxy-load-balancer).</span></span>

### <a name="webconfig-file"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-213">web.config 檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-213">web.config file</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-214">*web.config* 檔案是用來設定 [ASP.NET Core 模組](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-214">The *web.config* file configures the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-215">發佈專案時，由 MSBuild 目標 (`_TransformWebConfig`) 處理 *web.config* 檔案的建立、轉換及發佈。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-215">Creating, transforming, and publishing the *web.config* file is handled by an MSBuild target (`_TransformWebConfig`) when the project is published.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-216">此目標存在於 Web SDK 目標 (`Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-216">This target is present in the Web SDK targets (`Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-217">SDK 設定在專案檔的頂端：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-217">The SDK is set at the top of the project file:</span></span>

```xml
<Project Sdk="Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web">
```

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-218">如果專案中沒有 *web.config* 檔案，則系統會使用正確的 *processPath* 和 *arguments* 建立該檔案以設定 ASP.NET Core 模組，並將該檔案移至[已發行的輸出](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-218">If a *web.config* file isn't present in the project, the file is created with the correct *processPath* and *arguments* to configure the ASP.NET Core Module and moved to [published output](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-219">如果 *web.config* 檔案存在於專案中，則系統會使用正確的 *processPath* 和 *arguments* 來轉換該檔案以設定 ASP.NET Core 模組，然後將它移至已發行的輸出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-219">If a *web.config* file is present in the project, the file is transformed with the correct *processPath* and *arguments* to configure the ASP.NET Core Module and moved to published output.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-220">轉換不會修改檔案中的 IIS 組態設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-220">The transformation doesn't modify IIS configuration settings in the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-221">*web.config* 檔案可提供能控制作用中 IIS 模組的額外 IIS 組態設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-221">The *web.config* file may provide additional IIS configuration settings that control active IIS modules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-222">如需能處理 ASP.NET Core 應用程式要求之 IIS 模組的相關資訊，請參閱 [IIS 模組](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules)主題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-222">For information on IIS modules that are capable of processing requests with ASP.NET Core apps, see the [IIS modules](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules) topic.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-223">若要防止 Web SDK 轉換*web.config*檔案，請使用專案檔 **\<IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>** 中的屬性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-223">To prevent the Web SDK from transforming the *web.config* file, use the **\<IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>** property in the project file:</span></span>

```xml
<PropertyGroup>
  <IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>true</IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>
</PropertyGroup>
```

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-224">使 Web SDK 無法轉換檔案時，應該由開發人員手動設定 *processPath* 和 *arguments*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-224">When disabling the Web SDK from transforming the file, the *processPath* and *arguments* should be manually set by the developer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-225">如需詳細資訊，請參閱<xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-225">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

### <a name="webconfig-file-location"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-226">web.config 檔案位置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-226">web.config file location</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-227">為了正確設定[ASP.NET Core 模組](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module)， *web.config*檔案必須存在於[內容根](xref:fundamentals/index#content-root)路徑 (通常是已部署應用程式的應用程式基底路徑) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-227">In order to set up the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) correctly, the *web.config* file must be present at the [content root](xref:fundamentals/index#content-root) path (typically the app base path) of the deployed app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-228">這是與提供給 IIS 的網站實體路徑相同的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-228">This is the same location as the website physical path provided to IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-229">應用程式的根目錄需有 *web.config* 檔案，才能使用 Web Deploy 發行多個應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-229">The *web.config* file is required at the root of the app to enable the publishing of multiple apps using Web Deploy.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-230">機密檔案存在於應用程式的實體路徑上，例如\* \<assembly>.runtimeconfig.json*、 \* \<assembly> .xml* (xml 檔批註) ，以及\* \<assembly> 上的.deps.js\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-230">Sensitive files exist on the app's physical path, such as *\<assembly>.runtimeconfig.json*, *\<assembly>.xml* (XML Documentation comments), and *\<assembly>.deps.json*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-231">當 *web.config* 檔案存在且網站正常啟動時，如果有人要求機密檔案，IIS 不會予以提供。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-231">When the *web.config* file is present and the site starts normally, IIS doesn't serve these sensitive files if they're requested.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-232">若 *web.config* 檔案遺失或沒有正確命名，或是無法設定網站以正常啟動，IIS 可能會公開提供機密檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-232">If the *web.config* file is missing, incorrectly named, or unable to configure the site for normal startup, IIS may serve sensitive files publicly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-233">\***web.config*檔案必須隨時存在於部署中、正確命名，而且能夠將網站設定為正常啟動。絕對不要從生產環境部署移除*web.config\*檔案。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-233">**The *web.config* file must be present in the deployment at all times, correctly named, and able to configure the site for normal start up. Never remove the *web.config* file from a production deployment.**</span></span>

### <a name="transform-webconfig"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-234">轉換 web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-234">Transform web.config</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-235">如果您需要在發行時轉換*web.config* ，請參閱 <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/transform-webconfig> 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-235">If you need to transform *web.config* on publish, see <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/transform-webconfig>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-236">您可能需要在 [發行] 上轉換*web.config* ，以根據設定、設定檔或環境設定環境變數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-236">You might need to transform *web.config* on publish to set environment variables based on the configuration, profile, or environment.</span></span>

## <a name="iis-configuration"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-237">IIS 組態</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-237">IIS configuration</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-238">**Windows Server 作業系統**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-238">**Windows Server operating systems**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-239">啟用**網頁伺服器 (IIS)** 伺服器角色，並建立角色服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-239">Enable the **Web Server (IIS)** server role and establish role services.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-240">使用來自 [管理]\*\*\*\* 功能表的 [新增角色及功能]\*\*\*\* 精靈，或是 [伺服器管理員]\*\*\*\* 中的連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-240">Use the **Add Roles and Features** wizard from the **Manage** menu or the link in **Server Manager**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-241">在**伺服器角色**步驟中，核取 [網頁伺服器 (IIS)]\*\*\*\* 方塊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-241">On the **Server Roles** step, check the box for **Web Server (IIS)**.</span></span>

   ![在選取伺服器角色步驟中選取網頁伺服器 IIS 角色。](index/_static/server-roles-ws2016.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-243">在 [功能]\*\*\*\* 步驟之後，[角色服務]\*\*\*\* 步驟會針對網頁伺服器 (IIS) 進行載入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-243">After the **Features** step, the **Role services** step loads for Web Server (IIS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-244">選取所需的 IIS 角色服務或接受所提供的預設角色服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-244">Select the IIS role services desired or accept the default role services provided.</span></span>

   ![在選取角色服務步驟中，選取預設的角色服務。](index/_static/role-services-ws2016.png)

   <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-246">**Windows 驗證 (選擇性)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-246">**Windows Authentication (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-247">若要啟用 Windows 驗證，請展開下列節點： [**網頁伺服器**  >  **安全性**]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-247">To enable Windows Authentication, expand the following nodes: **Web Server** > **Security**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-248">選取 [Windows 驗證]\*\*\*\* 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-248">Select the **Windows Authentication** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-249">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[Windows 驗證 \<windowsAuthentication> ](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/)和[設定 windows 驗證](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-249">For more information, see [Windows Authentication \<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) and [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-250">**WebSocket (選擇性)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-250">**WebSockets (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-251">WebSocket 由 ASP.NET Core 1.1 或更新版本所支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-251">WebSockets is supported with ASP.NET Core 1.1 or later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-252">若要啟用 websocket，請展開下列節點： [**網頁伺服器**  >  **應用程式開發**]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-252">To enable WebSockets, expand the following nodes: **Web Server** > **Application Development**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-253">選取 [WebSocket 通訊協定]\*\*\*\* 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-253">Select the **WebSocket Protocol** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-254">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-254">For more information, see [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-255">透過**確認**步驟繼續作業，安裝網頁伺服器角色和服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-255">Proceed through the **Confirmation** step to install the web server role and services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-256">安裝\*\*Web 服務器 (iis) \*\*角色之後，不需要重新開機伺服器/iis。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-256">A server/IIS restart isn't required after installing the **Web Server (IIS)** role.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-257">**Windows 桌面作業系統**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-257">**Windows desktop operating systems**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-258">啟用 [IIS 管理主控台]\*\*\*\* 和 [World Wide Web 服務]\*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-258">Enable the **IIS Management Console** and **World Wide Web Services**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-259">瀏覽到 [控制台]\*\* [程式]\*\* > \*\* [程式和功能]\*\* > \*\*\*\* > **[開啟或關閉 Windows 功能]** \(畫面左側\)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-259">Navigate to **Control Panel** > **Programs** > **Programs and Features** > **Turn Windows features on or off** (left side of the screen).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-262">核取 [IIS 管理主控台]\*\*\*\* 方塊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-262">Check the box for **IIS Management Console**.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-265">**Windows 驗證 (選擇性)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-265">**Windows Authentication (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-266">若要啟用 Windows 驗證，請展開下列節點： **World Wide Web 服務**  >  **安全性**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-266">To enable Windows Authentication, expand the following nodes: **World Wide Web Services** > **Security**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-267">選取 [Windows 驗證]\*\*\*\* 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-267">Select the **Windows Authentication** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-268">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[Windows 驗證 \<windowsAuthentication> ](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/)和[設定 windows 驗證](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-268">For more information, see [Windows Authentication \<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) and [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-269">**WebSocket (選擇性)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-269">**WebSockets (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-270">WebSocket 由 ASP.NET Core 1.1 或更新版本所支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-270">WebSockets is supported with ASP.NET Core 1.1 or later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-271">若要啟用 websocket，請展開下列節點： [ **World Wide Web 服務**] [  >  **應用程式開發] 功能**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-271">To enable WebSockets, expand the following nodes: **World Wide Web Services** > **Application Development Features**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-272">選取 [WebSocket 通訊協定]\*\*\*\* 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-272">Select the **WebSocket Protocol** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-273">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-273">For more information, see [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span></span>

## <a name="install-the-net-core-hosting-bundle"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-276">安裝 .NET Core 裝載套件組合</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-276">Install the .NET Core Hosting Bundle</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-277">在主控系統上安裝 .NET Core 裝載套件組合\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-277">Install the *.NET Core Hosting Bundle* on the hosting system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-278">套件組合會安裝 .NET Core 執行時間、.NET Core 程式庫和[ASP.NET Core 模組](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-278">The bundle installs the .NET Core Runtime, .NET Core Library, and the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-279">此模組可讓 ASP.NET Core 應用程式在 IIS 背後執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-279">The module allows ASP.NET Core apps to run behind IIS.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-280">若裝載套件組合在 IIS 之前安裝，則必須對該套件組合安裝進行修復。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-280">If the Hosting Bundle is installed before IIS, the bundle installation must be repaired.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-281">請在安裝 IIS 之後，再次執行裝載套件組合安裝程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-281">Run the Hosting Bundle installer again after installing IIS.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-282">如果在安裝 64 位元 (x64) 版本的 .NET Core 後才安裝裝載套件組合，那麼可能會遺漏 SDK ([未偵測到 .NET Core SDK](xref:test/troubleshoot#no-net-core-sdks-were-detected))。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-282">If the Hosting Bundle is installed after installing the 64-bit (x64) version of .NET Core, SDKs might appear to be missing ([No .NET Core SDKs were detected](xref:test/troubleshoot#no-net-core-sdks-were-detected)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-283">若要解決此問題，請參閱 <xref:test/troubleshoot#missing-sdk-after-installing-the-net-core-hosting-bundle>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-283">To resolve the problem, see <xref:test/troubleshoot#missing-sdk-after-installing-the-net-core-hosting-bundle>.</span></span>

### <a name="earlier-versions-of-the-installer"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-287">安裝程式的先前版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-287">Earlier versions of the installer</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-288">若要取得安裝程式的先前版本：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-288">To obtain an earlier version of the installer:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-290">選取所需的 .NET Core 版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-290">Select the desired .NET Core version.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-291">在 [執行應用程式 - 執行階段]\*\*\*\* 欄中，尋找想要的 .NET Core 執行階段版本列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-291">In the **Run apps - Runtime** column, find the row of the .NET Core runtime version desired.</span></span>
