## <a name="locked-deployment-files"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-823">已鎖定的部署檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-823">Locked deployment files</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-824">當應用程式執行時，會鎖定部署資料夾中的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-824">Files in the deployment folder are locked when the app is running.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-825">無法於部署期間覆寫已鎖定的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-825">Locked files can't be overwritten during deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-826">若要釋放部署中的已鎖定檔案，請使用下列其中**一種**方法停止應用程式集區：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-826">To release locked files in a deployment, stop the app pool using **one** of the following approaches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-827">使用 Web Deploy 並參考專案檔中的 `Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-827">Use Web Deploy and reference `Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web` in the project file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-828">*app_offline.htm* 檔案是放在 Web 應用程式目錄的根目錄中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-828">An *app_offline.htm* file is placed at the root of the web app directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-829">當檔案存在時，ASP.NET Core 模組會正常關閉應用程式，並在部署期間提供 *app_offline.htm* 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-829">When the file is present, the ASP.NET Core Module gracefully shuts down the app and serves the *app_offline.htm* file during the deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-830">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [ASP.NET Core 模組組態參考](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#app_offlinehtm)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-830">For more information, see the [ASP.NET Core Module configuration reference](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#app_offlinehtm).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-831">在伺服器上的 IIS 管理員中手動停止應用程式集區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-831">Manually stop the app pool in the IIS Manager on the server.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-832">使用 PowerShell 捨棄*app_offline.htm* (需要 PowerShell 5 或更新版本) ：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-832">Use PowerShell to drop *app_offline.htm* (requires PowerShell 5 or later):</span></span>

  ```powershell
  $pathToApp = 'PATH_TO_APP'

  # Stop the AppPool
  New-Item -Path $pathToApp app_offline.htm

  # Provide script commands here to deploy the app

  # Restart the AppPool
  Remove-Item -Path $pathToApp app_offline.htm

  ```

## <a name="data-protection"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-833">資料保護</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-833">Data protection</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-834">[ASP.NET Core 資料保護堆疊](xref:security/data-protection/introduction)是由數個 ASP.NET Core [中介軟體](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index)所使用，包括用於驗證的中介軟體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-834">The [ASP.NET Core Data Protection stack](xref:security/data-protection/introduction) is used by several ASP.NET Core [middlewares](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index), including middleware used in authentication.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-835">即使資料保護 API 不是由使用者程式碼呼叫，仍應使用部署指令碼或是在使用者程式碼中設定資料保護，以建立持續性的密碼編譯[金鑰存放區](xref:security/data-protection/implementation/key-management)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-835">Even if Data Protection APIs aren't called by user code, data protection should be configured with a deployment script or in user code to create a persistent cryptographic [key store](xref:security/data-protection/implementation/key-management).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-836">如不設定資料保護，金鑰會保留在記憶體中，並於應用程式重新啟動時捨棄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-836">If data protection isn't configured, the keys are held in memory and discarded when the app restarts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-837">如果 Keyring 儲存在記憶體中，則當應用程式重新啟動時：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-837">If the key ring is stored in memory when the app restarts:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-838">所有架構 cookie 的驗證權杖都會失效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-838">All cookie-based authentication tokens are invalidated.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-839">當使用者提出下一個要求時，需要再次登入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-839">Users are required to sign in again on their next request.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-840">所有以 Keyring 保護的資料都無法再解密。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-840">Any data protected with the key ring can no longer be decrypted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-841">這可能包括[CSRF](xref:security/anti-request-forgery#aspnet-core-antiforgery-configuration) token 和[ASP.NET Core MVC TempData cookie s](xref:fundamentals/app-state#tempdata)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-841">This may include [CSRF tokens](xref:security/anti-request-forgery#aspnet-core-antiforgery-configuration) and [ASP.NET Core MVC TempData cookies](xref:fundamentals/app-state#tempdata).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-842">若要在 IIS 下設定資料保護以保存 Keyring，請使用下列其中**一種**方法：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-842">To configure data protection under IIS to persist the key ring, use **one** of the following approaches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-843">**建立資料保護登錄機碼**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-843">**Create Data Protection Registry Keys**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-844">ASP.NET Core 應用程式所使用的資料保護金鑰會儲存在應用程式外部的登錄中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-844">Data protection keys used by ASP.NET Core apps are stored in the registry external to the apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-845">若要保存指定應用程式的金鑰，請為應用程式集區建立登錄機碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-845">To persist the keys for a given app, create registry keys for the app pool.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-846">若為獨立的非Web 伺服陣列 IIS 安裝，請針對搭配使用 ASP.NET Core 應用程式的每個應用程式集區，使用[資料保護 Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1 PowerShell 指令碼](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/DataProtection/Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-846">For standalone, non-webfarm IIS installations, the [Data Protection Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1 PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/DataProtection/Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1) can be used for each app pool used with an ASP.NET Core app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-847">此指令碼會在 HKLM 登錄中建立登錄機碼，只有應用程式之應用程式集區的背景工作處理序帳戶可以存取它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-847">This script creates a registry key in the HKLM registry that's accessible only to the worker process account of the app's app pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-848">在待用期間使用 DPAPI 和全電腦金鑰加密金鑰。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-848">Keys are encrypted at rest using DPAPI with a machine-wide key.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-849">在 Web 伺服陣列案例中，應用程式可以設定成使用 UNC 路徑來儲存其資料保護 Keyring。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-849">In web farm scenarios, an app can be configured to use a UNC path to store its data protection key ring.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-850">根據預設，資料保護金鑰不予加密。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-850">By default, the data protection keys aren't encrypted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-851">請確保網路共用的檔案權限僅限於執行應用程式的 Windows 帳戶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-851">Ensure that the file permissions for the network share are limited to the Windows account the app runs under.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-852">可以使用 X509 憑證來保護待用的金鑰。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-852">An X509 certificate can be used to protect keys at rest.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-853">請考慮下列讓使用者上傳憑證的機制：將憑證放入使用者的受信任憑證存放區，並確保在執行使用者應用程式的所有電腦上都能使用這些憑證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-853">Consider a mechanism to allow users to upload certificates: Place certificates into the user's trusted certificate store and ensure they're available on all machines where the user's app runs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-854">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[設定 ASP.NET Core 資料保護](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-854">See [Configure ASP.NET Core Data Protection](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview) for details.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-855">**設定 IIS 應用程式集區載入使用者設定檔**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-855">**Configure the IIS Application Pool to load the user profile**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-856">此設定位在應用程式集區 [進階設定]\*\*\*\* 下的 [處理序模型]\*\*\*\* 區段中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-856">This setting is in the **Process Model** section under the **Advanced Settings** for the app pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-857">將 [載入使用者設定檔]\*\*\*\* 設為 `True`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-857">Set **Load User Profile** to `True`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-858">當設定為 `True` 時，金鑰會儲存在使用者設定檔目錄中，且使用具有使用者帳戶專屬金鑰的 DPAPI 保護。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-858">When set to `True`, keys are stored in the user profile directory and protected using DPAPI with a key specific to the user account.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-859">金鑰會保存到 *%LOCALAPPDATA%/ASP.NET/DataProtection-Keys* 資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-859">Keys are persisted to the *%LOCALAPPDATA%/ASP.NET/DataProtection-Keys* folder.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-860">應用程式集區的 [setProfileEnvironment 屬性](/iis/configuration/system.applicationhost/applicationpools/add/processmodel#configuration)也必須啟用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-860">The app pool's [setProfileEnvironment attribute](/iis/configuration/system.applicationhost/applicationpools/add/processmodel#configuration) must also be enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-861">`setProfileEnvironment` 的預設值為 `true`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-861">The default value of `setProfileEnvironment` is `true`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-862">在某些情況下 (例如 Windows OS)，`setProfileEnvironment` 會設為 `false`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-862">In some scenarios (for example, Windows OS), `setProfileEnvironment` is set to `false`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-863">如果金鑰並未如預期地儲存在使用者設定檔目錄中：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-863">If keys aren't stored in the user profile directory as expected:</span></span>

  1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-864">瀏覽至 *%windir%/system32/inetsrv/config* 資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-864">Navigate to the *%windir%/system32/inetsrv/config* folder.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-865">開啟 *applicationHost.config* 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-865">Open the *applicationHost.config* file.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-866">找出 `<system.applicationHost><applicationPools><applicationPoolDefaults><processModel>` 元素。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-866">Locate the `<system.applicationHost><applicationPools><applicationPoolDefaults><processModel>` element.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-867">確認 `setProfileEnvironment` 屬性不存在 (其預設值為 `true`)，或明確地將屬性值設為 `true`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-867">Confirm that the `setProfileEnvironment` attribute isn't present, which defaults the value to `true`, or explicitly set the attribute's value to `true`.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-868">**將檔案系統當作 Keyring 存放區使用**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-868">**Use the file system as a key ring store**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-869">調整應用程式程式碼，以[將檔案系統當作 Keyring 存放區使用](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-869">Adjust the app code to [use the file system as a key ring store](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-870">使用 X509 憑證來保護 Keyring，並確保憑證是受信任的憑證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-870">Use an X509 certificate to protect the key ring and ensure the certificate is a trusted certificate.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-871">如果憑證為自我簽署，請將憑證放在受信任的根存放區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-871">If the certificate is self-signed, place the certificate in the Trusted Root store.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-872">在 Web 伺服陣列中使用 IIS 時：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-872">When using IIS in a web farm:</span></span>

  * <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-873">請使用所有電腦都可以存取的檔案共用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-873">Use a file share that all machines can access.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-874">將 X509 憑證部署到每一部電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-874">Deploy an X509 certificate to each machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-875">設定[程式碼中的資料保護](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-875">Configure [data protection in code](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview).</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-876">**設定資料保護的全電腦原則**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-876">**Set a machine-wide policy for data protection**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-877">針對取用資料保護 API 的所有應用程式，資料保護系統僅支援有限的預設[全電腦原則](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/machine-wide-policy)設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-877">The data protection system has limited support for setting a default [machine-wide policy](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/machine-wide-policy) for all apps that consume the Data Protection APIs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-878">如需詳細資訊，請參閱<xref:security/data-protection/introduction>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-878">For more information, see <xref:security/data-protection/introduction>.</span></span>

## <a name="virtual-directories"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-879">虛擬目錄</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-879">Virtual Directories</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-880">ASP.NET Core 應用程式不支援 [IIS 虛擬目錄](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#virtual-directories)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-880">[IIS Virtual Directories](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#virtual-directories) aren't supported with ASP.NET Core apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-881">應用程式能以[子應用程式](#sub-applications)的形式裝載。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-881">An app can be hosted as a [sub-application](#sub-applications).</span></span>

## <a name="sub-applications"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-882">子應用程式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-882">Sub-applications</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-883">ASP.NET Core 應用程式能以 [IIS 子應用程式](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#applications)的形式裝載。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-883">An ASP.NET Core app can be hosted as an [IIS sub-application (sub-app)](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#applications).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-884">子應用程式的路徑會成為根應用程式 URL 的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-884">The sub-app's path becomes part of the root app's URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-885">子應用程式內的靜態資產連結應該使用波狀符號與斜線 (`~/`) 標記法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-885">Static asset links within the sub-app should use tilde-slash (`~/`) notation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-886">波狀符號與斜線標記法會觸發[標記協助程式](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro)以將子應用程式的路徑基底附加到轉譯的相對連結前面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-886">Tilde-slash notation triggers a [Tag Helper](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro) to prepend the sub-app's pathbase to the rendered relative link.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-887">針對位於 `/subapp_path` 的子應用程式，使用 `src="~/image.png"` 連結的影像會轉譯為 `src="/subapp_path/image.png"`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-887">For a sub-app at `/subapp_path`, an image linked with `src="~/image.png"` is rendered as `src="/subapp_path/image.png"`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-888">根應用程式的靜態檔案中介軟體不會處理靜態檔案要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-888">The root app's Static File Middleware doesn't process the static file request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-889">要求會由子應用程式的靜態檔案中介軟體處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-889">The request is processed by the sub-app's Static File Middleware.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-890">若靜態資產的 `src` 屬性是設定為絕對路徑 (例如，`src="/image.png"`)，會以不使用子應用程式路徑基底的方式轉譯連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-890">If a static asset's `src` attribute is set to an absolute path (for example, `src="/image.png"`), the link is rendered without the sub-app's pathbase.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-891">根應用程式的靜態檔案中介軟體會嘗試從根應用程式的 [webroot](xref:fundamentals/index#web-root) 提供資產，這會導致「404 - 找不到」\*\* 回應 (除非根應用程式可存取靜態資產)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-891">The root app's Static File Middleware attempts to serve the asset from the root app's [web root](xref:fundamentals/index#web-root), which results in a *404 - Not Found* response unless the static asset is available from the root app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-892">裝載 ASP.NET Core 應用程式做為另一個 ASP.NET Core 應用程式下的子應用程式：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-892">To host an ASP.NET Core app as a sub-app under another ASP.NET Core app:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-893">為子應用程式建立應用程式集區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-893">Establish an app pool for the sub-app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-894">將 [.NET CLR 版本]\*\*\*\* 設定為 [沒有受控碼]\*\*\*\*，因為會將核心通用語言執行平台 (CoreCLR) 開機以在背景工作處理序中裝載應用程式，而非在桌面 CLR (.NET CLR) 中裝載。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-894">Set the **.NET CLR Version** to **No Managed Code** because the Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) for .NET Core is booted to host the app in the worker process, not the desktop CLR (.NET CLR).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-895">使用根網站下資料夾中的子應用程式在 IIS 管理員中新增根網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-895">Add the root site in IIS Manager with the sub-app in a folder under the root site.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-896">以滑鼠右鍵按一下 IIS 管理員中的子應用程式資料夾，然後選取 [轉換成應用程式]\*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-896">Right-click the sub-app folder in IIS Manager and select **Convert to Application**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-897">在 [新增應用程式]\*\*\*\* 對話方塊中，使用 [應用程式集區]\*\*\*\* 的[選取]\*\*\*\* 按鈕來指派您為子應用程式建立的應用程式集區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-897">In the **Add Application** dialog, use the **Select** button for the **Application Pool** to assign the app pool that you created for the sub-app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-898">選取 [確定]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-898">Select **OK**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-899">將不同的應用程式集區指派給子應用程式是使用同處理序裝載模型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-899">The assignment of a separate app pool to the sub-app is a requirement when using the in-process hosting model.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-900">如需有關同進程裝載模型和設定 ASP.NET Core 模組的詳細資訊，請參閱 <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module> 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-900">For more information on the in-process hosting model and configuring the ASP.NET Core Module, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

## <a name="configuration-of-iis-with-webconfig"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-901">使用 web.config 的 IIS 組態</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-901">Configuration of IIS with web.config</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-902">在對使用了 ASP.NET Core 模組的 ASP.NET Core 有作用的 IIS 情境下，設定會受 *web.config* 的 `<system.webServer>` 區段影響。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-902">IIS configuration is influenced by the `<system.webServer>` section of *web.config* for IIS scenarios that are functional for ASP.NET Core apps with the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-903">舉例來說，IIS 設定對動態壓縮有作用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-903">For example, IIS configuration is functional for dynamic compression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-904">如果在伺服器層級將 IIS 設為使用動態壓縮，應用程式 *web.config* 檔案中的 `<urlCompression>` 元素則可為 ASP.NET Core 應用程式予以停用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-904">If IIS is configured at the server level to use dynamic compression, the `<urlCompression>` element in the app's *web.config* file can disable it for an ASP.NET Core app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-905">如需詳細資訊，請參閱下列主題：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-905">For more information, see the following topics:</span></span>

* [<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-906">的設定參考\<system.webServer></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-906">Configuration reference for \<system.webServer></span></span>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/)
* <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>
* <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-907">若要設定在隔離的應用程式集區中執行之個別應用程式的環境變數 (支援 IIS 10.0 或更新版本) ，請參閱 IIS 參考檔中[環境變數 \<environmentVariables> ](/iis/configuration/system.applicationHost/applicationPools/add/environmentVariables/#appcmdexe)主題的*AppCmd.exe 命令*一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-907">To set environment variables for individual apps running in isolated app pools (supported for IIS 10.0 or later), see the *AppCmd.exe command* section of the [Environment Variables \<environmentVariables>](/iis/configuration/system.applicationHost/applicationPools/add/environmentVariables/#appcmdexe) topic in the IIS reference documentation.</span></span>

## <a name="configuration-sections-of-webconfig"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-908">web.config 的組態區段</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-908">Configuration sections of web.config</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-909">ASP.NET Core 應用程式的設定不使用 *web.config* 中 ASP.NET 4.x 應用程式的設定區段：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-909">Configuration sections of ASP.NET 4.x apps in *web.config* aren't used by ASP.NET Core apps for configuration:</span></span>

* `<system.web>`
* `<appSettings>`
* `<connectionStrings>`
* `<location>`

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-910">使用其他組態提供者設定的 ASP.NET Core 應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-910">ASP.NET Core apps are configured using other configuration providers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-911">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[Configuration](xref:fundamentals/configuration/index)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-911">For more information, see [Configuration](xref:fundamentals/configuration/index).</span></span>

## <a name="application-pools"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-912">應用程式集區</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-912">Application Pools</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-913">應用程式集區隔離取決於裝載模型：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-913">App pool isolation is determined by the hosting model:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-914">同進程裝載：應用程式必須在不同的應用程式集區中執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-914">In-process hosting: Apps are required to run in separate app pools.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-915">跨進程裝載：我們建議您在自己的應用程式集區中執行每個應用程式，以將應用程式彼此隔離。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-915">Out-of-process hosting: We recommend isolating the apps from each other by running each app in its own app pool.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-916">IIS [新增網站]\*\*\*\* 對話方塊預設每個應用程式皆為單一應用程式集區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-916">The IIS **Add Website** dialog defaults to a single app pool per app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-917">當提供**網站名稱**時，文字會自動轉移至 [應用程式集區]\*\*\*\* 文字方塊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-917">When a **Site name** is provided, the text is automatically transferred to the **Application pool** textbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-918">新增網站時，會使用該網站名稱建立新的應用程式集區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-918">A new app pool is created using the site name when the site is added.</span></span>

## <a name="application-pool-no-locidentity"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-919">應用程式集區Identity</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-919">Application Pool Identity</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-920">應用程式集區身分識別帳戶可讓應用程式在唯一的帳戶下執行，不必建立及管理網域或本機帳戶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-920">An app pool identity account allows an app to run under a unique account without having to create and manage domains or local accounts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-921">在 IIS 8.0 或更新版本中，IIS 管理背景工作處理序 (WAS) 會使用新的應用程式集區名稱建立虛擬帳戶，並預設在此帳戶下執行應用程式集區的背景工作處理序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-921">On IIS 8.0 or later, the IIS Admin Worker Process (WAS) creates a virtual account with the name of the new app pool and runs the app pool's worker processes under this account by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-922">在 IIS 管理主控台中，于應用程式集區的 [**高級設定**] 底下，確定 **Identity** 已設定為使用\*\*ApplicationPool Identity \*\*：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-922">In the IIS Management Console under **Advanced Settings** for the app pool, ensure that the **Identity** is set to use **ApplicationPoolIdentity**:</span></span>

![應用程式集區進階設定對話方塊](index/_static/apppool-identity.png)

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-924">IIS 管理程序會在 Windows 安全系統中，以應用程式集區的名稱建立安全識別碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-924">The IIS management process creates a secure identifier with the name of the app pool in the Windows Security System.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-925">可使用此身分識別來保護資源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-925">Resources can be secured using this identity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-926">不過，此身分識別不是真正的使用者帳戶，也不會顯示在 Windows 使用者管理主控台中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-926">However, this identity isn't a real user account and doesn't show up in the Windows User Management Console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-927">如果 IIS 背景工作處理序需要提升應用程式的存取權限，請修改包含應用程式的目錄存取控制清單 (ACL)：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-927">If the IIS worker process requires elevated access to the app, modify the Access Control List (ACL) for the directory containing the app:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-928">開啟 Windows 檔案總管，巡覽至目錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-928">Open Windows Explorer and navigate to the directory.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-929">以滑鼠右鍵按一下目錄並選取 [屬性]\*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-929">Right-click on the directory and select **Properties**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-930">依序選取 [安全性]\*\*\*\* 索引標籤下的 [編輯]\*\*\*\* 按鈕和 [新增]\*\*\*\* 按鈕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-930">Under the **Security** tab, select the **Edit** button and then the **Add** button.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-931">選取 [位置]\*\*\*\* 按鈕，並確定選取系統。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-931">Select the **Locations** button and make sure the system is selected.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-932">在 [輸入要選取的物件名稱]\*\*\*\* 區域中，輸入 **IIS AppPool\\<app_pool_name>**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-932">Enter **IIS AppPool\\<app_pool_name>** in **Enter the object names to select** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-933">選取 [檢查名稱]\*\*\*\* 按鈕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-933">Select the **Check Names** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-934">針對 [DefaultAppPool]\*\*，請使用 **IIS AppPool\DefaultAppPool** 檢查名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-934">For the *DefaultAppPool* check the names using **IIS AppPool\DefaultAppPool**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-935">選取 [檢查名稱]\*\*\*\* 按鈕時，[DefaultAppPool]\*\*\*\* 的值便會顯示於物件名稱區域中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-935">When the **Check Names** button is selected, a value of **DefaultAppPool** is indicated in the object names area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-936">您無法直接將應用程式集區名稱輸入至物件名稱區域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-936">It isn't possible to enter the app pool name directly into the object names area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-937">檢查物件名稱時，請使用 **IIS AppPool\\<app_pool_name>** 的格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-937">Use the **IIS AppPool\\<app_pool_name>** format when checking for the object name.</span></span>

   ![針對應用程式資料夾選取使用者或群組對話方塊：在選取 [檢查名稱] 之前，"DefaultAppPool" 這個應用程式集區名稱在物件名稱區域中會附加至 "IIS AppPool\"。](index/_static/select-users-or-groups-1.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-939">選取 [確定]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-939">Select **OK**.</span></span>

   ![針對應用程式資料夾選取使用者或群組對話方塊：選取 [檢查名稱] 之後，物件名稱 "DefaultAppPool" 會顯示在物件名稱區域中。](index/_static/select-users-or-groups-2.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-941">預設應該會授與讀取 &amp; 執行權限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-941">Read &amp; execute permissions should be granted by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-942">請視需要提供其他權限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-942">Provide additional permissions as needed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-943">也可使用 **ICACLS** 工具透過命令提示字元授與存取權限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-943">Access can also be granted at a command prompt using the **ICACLS** tool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-944">使用 *DefaultAppPool*作為範例，將會使用下列命令：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-944">Using the *DefaultAppPool* as an example, the following command is used:</span></span>

```console
ICACLS C:\sites\MyWebApp /grant "IIS AppPool\DefaultAppPool":F
```

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-945">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [icacls](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/icacls) 主題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-945">For more information, see the [icacls](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/icacls) topic.</span></span>

## <a name="http2-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-946">HTTP/2 支援</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-946">HTTP/2 support</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-947">在下列 IIS 部署案例中，ASP.NET Core 支援 [HTTP/2](https://httpwg.org/specs/rfc7540.html)：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-947">[HTTP/2](https://httpwg.org/specs/rfc7540.html) is supported with ASP.NET Core in the following IIS deployment scenarios:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-948">內含式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-948">In-process</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-949">Windows Server 2016/Windows 10 或更新版本；IIS 10 或更新版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-949">Windows Server 2016/Windows 10 or later; IIS 10 or later</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-950">TLS 1.2 或更新版本連線</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-950">TLS 1.2 or later connection</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-951">跨處理序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-951">Out-of-process</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-952">Windows Server 2016/Windows 10 或更新版本；IIS 10 或更新版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-952">Windows Server 2016/Windows 10 or later; IIS 10 or later</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-953">公開 Edge Server 連線使用 HTTP/2，但是對 [Kestrel 伺服器](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel)的反向 Proxy 連線使用 HTTP/1.1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-953">Public-facing edge server connections use HTTP/2, but the reverse proxy connection to the [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel) uses HTTP/1.1.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-954">TLS 1.2 或更新版本連線</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-954">TLS 1.2 or later connection</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-955">針對建立 HTTP/2 連線時的同處理序部署，[HttpRequest.Protocol](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.Protocol*) 會回報 `HTTP/2`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-955">For an in-process deployment when an HTTP/2 connection is established, [HttpRequest.Protocol](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.Protocol*) reports `HTTP/2`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-956">針對建立 HTTP/2 連線時的跨處理序部署，[HttpRequest.Protocol](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.Protocol*) 會回報 `HTTP/1.1`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-956">For an out-of-process deployment when an HTTP/2 connection is established, [HttpRequest.Protocol](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.Protocol*) reports `HTTP/1.1`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-957">如需有關同處理序和跨處理序主控模型的詳細資訊，請參閱 <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-957">For more information on the in-process and out-of-process hosting models, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-958">HTTP/2 預設為啟用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-958">HTTP/2 is enabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-959">如果 HTTP/2 連線尚未建立，連線會退為 HTTP/1.1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-959">Connections fall back to HTTP/1.1 if an HTTP/2 connection isn't established.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-960">如需使用 IIS 部署之 HTTP/2 設定的詳細資訊，請參閱 [IIS 上的 HTTP/2](/iis/get-started/whats-new-in-iis-10/http2-on-iis)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-960">For more information on HTTP/2 configuration with IIS deployments, see [HTTP/2 on IIS](/iis/get-started/whats-new-in-iis-10/http2-on-iis).</span></span>

## <a name="cors-preflight-requests"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-961">CORS 預檢要求</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-961">CORS preflight requests</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-962">*此節只適用於以 .NET Framework 為目標的 ASP.NET Core 應用程式。*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-962">*This section only applies to ASP.NET Core apps that target the .NET Framework.*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-963">針對以 .NET Framework 為目標的 ASP.NET Core 應用程式，在 IIS 中OPTIONS 要求預設不會傳遞到應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-963">For an ASP.NET Core app that targets the .NET Framework, OPTIONS requests aren't passed to the app by default in IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-964">若要瞭解如何在*web.config*中設定應用程式的 IIS 處理常式以傳遞選項要求，請參閱[在 ASP.NET Web API 2 中啟用跨原始來源要求： CORS 的運作方式](/aspnet/web-api/overview/security/enabling-cross-origin-requests-in-web-api#how-cors-works)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-964">To learn how to configure the app's IIS handlers in *web.config* to pass OPTIONS requests, see [Enable cross-origin requests in ASP.NET Web API 2: How CORS Works](/aspnet/web-api/overview/security/enabling-cross-origin-requests-in-web-api#how-cors-works).</span></span>

## <a name="application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-965">應用程式初始化模組與閒置逾時</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-965">Application Initialization Module and Idle Timeout</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-966">在 IIS 中由 ASP.NET Core 模組版本 2 裝載時：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-966">When hosted in IIS by the ASP.NET Core Module version 2:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-967">[應用程式初始化模組](#application-initialization-module)：應用程式裝載的同[進程](#in-process-hosting-model)或跨[進程](#out-of-process-hosting-model)可以設定為在背景工作進程重新開機或伺服器重新開機時自動啟動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-967">[Application Initialization Module](#application-initialization-module): App's hosted [in-process](#in-process-hosting-model) or [out-of-process](#out-of-process-hosting-model) can be configured to start automatically on a worker process restart or server restart.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-968">[閒置超時](#idle-timeout)：應用程式的裝載同[進程](#in-process-hosting-model)可以設定為不在非活動期間的時間超時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-968">[Idle Timeout](#idle-timeout): App's hosted [in-process](#in-process-hosting-model) can be configured not to timeout during periods of inactivity.</span></span>

### <a name="application-initialization-module"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-969">應用程式初始化模組</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-969">Application Initialization Module</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-970">*套用到應用程式裝載同處理序與非同處理序。*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-970">*Applies to apps hosted in-process and out-of-process.*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-971">[IIS 應用程式初始化](/iis/get-started/whats-new-in-iis-8/iis-80-application-initialization)是一項 IIS 功能，可在應用程式集區啟動或回收時，將 HTTP 要求傳送給應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-971">[IIS Application Initialization](/iis/get-started/whats-new-in-iis-8/iis-80-application-initialization) is an IIS feature that sends an HTTP request to the app when the app pool starts or is recycled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-972">要求會觸發應用程式啟動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-972">The request triggers the app to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-973">根據預設，IIS 會發出應用程式根 URL (`/`) 的要求以初始化應用程式 (如需有關設定的詳細資訊，請參閱[額外資源](#application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout-additional-resources))。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-973">By default, IIS issues a request to the app's root URL (`/`) to initialize the app (see the [additional resources](#application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout-additional-resources) for more details on configuration).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-974">確認已啟用「IIS 應用程式初始化」角色功能：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-974">Confirm that the IIS Application Initialization role feature in enabled:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-975">在 Windows 7 或更新的電腦系統上，當在本機使用 IIS 時：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-975">On Windows 7 or later desktop systems when using IIS locally:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-976">瀏覽到 [控制台]\*\* [程式]\*\* > \*\* [程式和功能]\*\* > \*\*\*\* > **[開啟或關閉 Windows 功能]** \(畫面左側\)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-976">Navigate to **Control Panel** > **Programs** > **Programs and Features** > **Turn Windows features on or off** (left side of the screen).</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-977">開啟 [網際網路資訊服務]\*\* [World Wide Web 服務]\*\* > \*\* [應用程式開發功能]\*\* > \*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-977">Open **Internet Information Services** > **World Wide Web Services** > **Application Development Features**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-978">選取 [應用程式初始化]\*\*\*\* 的核取方塊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-978">Select the check box for **Application Initialization**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-979">在 Windows Server 2008 R2 或更新版本上：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-979">On Windows Server 2008 R2 or later:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-980">開啟「新增角色與功能精靈」\*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-980">Open the **Add Roles and Features Wizard**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-981">在 [選取角色服務]\*\*\*\* 面板中，開啟 [應用程式開發]\*\*\*\* 節點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-981">In the **Select role services** panel, open the **Application Development** node.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-982">選取 [應用程式初始化]\*\*\*\* 的核取方塊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-982">Select the check box for **Application Initialization**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-983">使用下列任一方式為網站啟用應用程式初始化模組：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-983">Use either of the following approaches to enable the Application Initialization Module for the site:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-984">使用 IIS 管理員：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-984">Using IIS Manager:</span></span>

  1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-985">選取 [連線]\*\*\*\* 面板中的 [應用程式集區]\*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-985">Select **Application Pools** in the **Connections** panel.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-986">以滑鼠右鍵按一下清單中應用程式的應用程式集區，然後選取 [進階設定]\*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-986">Right-click the app's app pool in the list and select **Advanced Settings**.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-987">預設的 [啟動模式]\*\*\*\* 是 [OnDemand]\*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-987">The default **Start Mode** is **OnDemand**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-988">將 [啟動模式]\*\*\*\* 設定為 [AlwaysRunning]\*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-988">Set the **Start Mode** to **AlwaysRunning**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-989">選取 [確定]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-989">Select **OK**.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-990">開啟 [連線]\*\*\*\* 面板中的 [站台]\*\*\*\* 節點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-990">Open the **Sites** node in the **Connections** panel.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-991">以滑鼠右鍵按一下應用程式，然後選取 [管理網站]\*\* [進階設定]\*\* > \*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-991">Right-click the app and select **Manage Website** > **Advanced Settings**.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-992">預設 [預先載入已啟用]\*\*\*\* 設定是 [False]\*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-992">The default **Preload Enabled** setting is **False**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-993">將 [預先載入已啟用]\*\*\*\* 設定為 [True]\*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-993">Set **Preload Enabled** to **True**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-994">選取 [確定]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-994">Select **OK**.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-995">使用 *web.config*，新增 `<applicationInitialization>` 元素並將 `doAppInitAfterRestart` 設定為 `true` 至應用程式 *web.config* 檔案中的 `<system.webServer>` 元素：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-995">Using *web.config*, add the `<applicationInitialization>` element with `doAppInitAfterRestart` set to `true` to the `<system.webServer>` elements in the app's *web.config* file:</span></span>

  ```xml
  <?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
  <configuration>
    <location path="." inheritInChildApplications="false">
      <system.webServer>
        <applicationInitialization doAppInitAfterRestart="true" />
      </system.webServer>
    </location>
  </configuration>
  ```

### <a name="idle-timeout"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-996">閒置逾時</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-996">Idle Timeout</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-997">*僅適用於應用程式裝載同處理序。*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-997">*Only applies to apps hosted in-process.*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-998">若要防止應用程式閒置，請使用 IIS 管理員設定應用程式集區的閒置逾時：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-998">To prevent the app from idling, set the app pool's idle timeout using IIS Manager:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-999">選取 [連線]\*\*\*\* 面板中的 [應用程式集區]\*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-999">Select **Application Pools** in the **Connections** panel.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1000">以滑鼠右鍵按一下清單中應用程式的應用程式集區，然後選取 [進階設定]\*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1000">Right-click the app's app pool in the list and select **Advanced Settings**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1001">預設 [閒置逾時 (分鐘)]\*\*\*\* 是 **20** 分鐘。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1001">The default **Idle Time-out (minutes)** is **20** minutes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1002">將 [閒置逾時 (分鐘)]\*\*\*\* 設定為 **0** (零)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1002">Set the **Idle Time-out (minutes)** to **0** (zero).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1003">選取 [確定]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1003">Select **OK**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1004">回收背景工作處理序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1004">Recycle the worker process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1005">若要防止應用程式裝載[非同處理序](#out-of-process-hosting-model)逾時，請使用下列任一方式：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1005">To prevent apps hosted [out-of-process](#out-of-process-hosting-model) from timing out, use either of the following approaches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1006">從外部服務對應用程式執行 Ping 以讓它繼續執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1006">Ping the app from an external service in order to keep it running.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1007">若應用程式只裝載背景服務，避免 IIS 裝載並使用 [Windows 服務來裝載 ASP.NET Core 應用程式](xref:host-and-deploy/windows-service)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1007">If the app only hosts background services, avoid IIS hosting and use a [Windows Service to host the ASP.NET Core app](xref:host-and-deploy/windows-service).</span></span>

### <a name="application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout-additional-resources"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1008">應用程式初始化模組與閒置逾時額外資源</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1008">Application Initialization Module and Idle Timeout additional resources</span></span>
