## <a name="supported-operating-systems"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1022">支援的作業系統</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1022">Supported operating systems</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1023">以下為支援的作業系統：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1023">The following operating systems are supported:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1024">Windows 7 或更新版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1024">Windows 7 or later</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1025">Windows Server 2008 R2 或更新版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1025">Windows Server 2008 R2 or later</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1026">[HTTP.sys 伺服器](xref:fundamentals/servers/httpsys) (先前稱為 WebListener) 不適用搭配 IIS 的反向 Proxy 設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1026">[HTTP.sys server](xref:fundamentals/servers/httpsys) (formerly called WebListener) doesn't work in a reverse proxy configuration with IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1027">請使用 [Kestrel 伺服器](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1027">Use the [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1028">如需在 Azure 中裝載的資訊，請參閱 <xref:host-and-deploy/azure-apps/index>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1028">For information on hosting in Azure, see <xref:host-and-deploy/azure-apps/index>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1029">如需疑難排解指引，請參閱 <xref:test/troubleshoot>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1029">For troubleshooting guidance, see <xref:test/troubleshoot>.</span></span>

## <a name="supported-platforms"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1030">支援的平台</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1030">Supported platforms</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1031">支援針對 32 位元 (x86) 或 64 位元 (x64) 部署發行的應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1031">Apps published for 32-bit (x86) or 64-bit (x64) deployment are supported.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1032">使用 32 位元 (x86) .NET Core SDK 部署 32 位元應用程式，除非應用程式：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1032">Deploy a 32-bit app with a 32-bit (x86) .NET Core SDK unless the app:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1033">需要提供給 64 位元應用程式使用的較大虛擬記憶體位址空間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1033">Requires the larger virtual memory address space available to a 64-bit app.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1034">需要較大的 IIS 堆疊大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1034">Requires the larger IIS stack size.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1035">有 64 位元原生相依性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1035">Has 64-bit native dependencies.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1036">使用 64 位元 (x64) .NET Core SDK 來發行 64 位元應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1036">Use a 64-bit (x64) .NET Core SDK to publish a 64-bit app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1037">主機系統上必須有 64 位元執行階段存在。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1037">A 64-bit runtime must be present on the host system.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1038">ASP.NET Core 隨附 [Kestrel 伺服器](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel)，其為預設的跨平台 HTTP 伺服器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1038">ASP.NET Core ships with [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel), a default, cross-platform HTTP server.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1039">在使用 [IIS](/iis/get-started/introduction-to-iis/introduction-to-iis-architecture) 或 [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) 時，應用程式會執行於從 IIS 背景工作處理序中分離出的處理序 (跨處理序\*\*)，並搭配 [Kestrel 伺服器](xref:fundamentals/servers/index#kestrel)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1039">When using [IIS](/iis/get-started/introduction-to-iis/introduction-to-iis-architecture) or [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview), the app runs in a process separate from the IIS worker process (*out-of-process*) with the [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/index#kestrel).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1040">因為 ASP.NET Core 應用程式執行所在的處理序會與 IIS 工作者處理序分開，所以此模組會執行處理程序管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1040">Because ASP.NET Core apps run in a process separate from the IIS worker process, the module handles process management.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1041">此模組會在第一個要求到達時啟動 ASP.NET Core 應用程式的處理序，並在應用程式關閉或損毀時將它重新啟動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1041">The module starts the process for the ASP.NET Core app when the first request arrives and restarts the app if it shuts down or crashes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1042">此行為基本上與執行同處理序，並由 [Windows 處理序啟用服務 (WAS)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was) 所管理的應用程式相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1042">This is essentially the same behavior as seen with apps that run in-process that are managed by the [Windows Process Activation Service (WAS)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1043">下圖說明 IIS、ASP.NET Core 模組和跨處理序裝載應用程式之間的關聯性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1043">The following diagram illustrates the relationship between IIS, the ASP.NET Core Module, and an app hosted out-of-process:</span></span>

![ASP.NET Core 模組](index/_static/ancm-outofprocess.png)

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1045">要求會從 Web 到達核心模式的 HTTP.sys 驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1045">Requests arrive from the web to the kernel-mode HTTP.sys driver.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1046">驅動程式會在網站設定的通訊埠上將要求路由至 IIS，此通訊埠通常是 80 (HTTP) 或 443 (HTTPS)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1046">The driver routes the requests to IIS on the website's configured port, usually 80 (HTTP) or 443 (HTTPS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1047">此模組會在應用程式的隨機通訊埠上將要求轉送至 Kestrel，而且不會是通訊埠 80 或 443。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1047">The module forwards the requests to Kestrel on a random port for the app, which isn't port 80 or 443.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1048">此模組會在啟動時透過環境變數指定埠，而[IIS 整合中介軟體](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#enable-the-iisintegration-components)會設定伺服器來接聽 `http://localhost:{port}` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1048">The module specifies the port via an environment variable at startup, and the [IIS Integration Middleware](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#enable-the-iisintegration-components) configures the server to listen on `http://localhost:{port}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1049">將會執行額外檢查，不是源自模組的要求都會遭到拒絕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1049">Additional checks are performed, and requests that don't originate from the module are rejected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1050">此模組不支援 HTTPS 轉送，因此即使由 IIS 透過 HTTPS 接收，要求還是會透過 HTTP 轉送。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1050">The module doesn't support HTTPS forwarding, so requests are forwarded over HTTP even if received by IIS over HTTPS.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1051">Kestrel 收取來自模組的要求之後，要求會被推送至 ASP.NET Core 中介軟體管線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1051">After Kestrel picks up the request from the module, the request is pushed into the ASP.NET Core middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1052">中介軟體管線會處理要求，並將其作為 `HttpContext` 執行個體傳遞至應用程式的邏輯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1052">The middleware pipeline handles the request and passes it on as an `HttpContext` instance to the app's logic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1053">IIS Integration 新增的中介軟體會更新配置、遠端 IP 和帳戶路徑基底，以將要求轉送至 Kestrel。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1053">Middleware added by IIS Integration updates the scheme, remote IP, and pathbase to account for forwarding the request to Kestrel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1054">應用程式的回應會傳回 IIS，而 IIS 會將其推送回起始要求的 HTTP 用戶端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1054">The app's response is passed back to IIS, which pushes it back out to the HTTP client that initiated the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1055">`CreateDefaultBuilder` 會將 [Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel) 伺服器設為網頁伺服器，並設定 [ASP.NET Core 模組](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module)的基底路徑與連接埠來啟用 IIS 整合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1055">`CreateDefaultBuilder` configures [Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel) server as the web server and enables IIS Integration by configuring the base path and port for the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1056">ASP.NET Core 模組會產生要指派給後端處理序的動態連接埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1056">The ASP.NET Core Module generates a dynamic port to assign to the backend process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1057">`CreateDefaultBuilder` 會呼叫 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIISIntegration*> 方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1057">`CreateDefaultBuilder` calls the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIISIntegration*> method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1058">`UseIISIntegration` 會將 Kestrel 設定為在位於 localhost IP 位址 (`127.0.0.1`) 的動態連接埠上接聽。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1058">`UseIISIntegration` configures Kestrel to listen on the dynamic port at the localhost IP address (`127.0.0.1`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1059">若動態連接埠是 1234，Kestrel 會在 `127.0.0.1:1234` 接聽。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1059">If the dynamic port is 1234, Kestrel listens at `127.0.0.1:1234`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1060">此設定會取代由下列項目提供的其他 URL 設定：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1060">This configuration replaces other URL configurations provided by:</span></span>

* `UseUrls`
* [<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1061">Kestrel 的接聽 API</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1061">Kestrel's Listen API</span></span>](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel#endpoint-configuration)
* <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1062">[設定](xref:fundamentals/configuration/index) (或[命令列 --urls 選項](xref:fundamentals/host/web-host#override-configuration))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1062">[Configuration](xref:fundamentals/configuration/index) (or [command-line --urls option](xref:fundamentals/host/web-host#override-configuration))</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1063">在使用模組時不需要呼叫 `UseUrls` 或 Kestrel 的 `Listen` API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1063">Calls to `UseUrls` or Kestrel's `Listen` API aren't required when using the module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1064">若呼叫 `UseUrls` 或 `Listen`，Kestrel 只會接聽未使用 IIS 執行應用程式時指定的連接埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1064">If `UseUrls` or `Listen` is called, Kestrel listens on the port specified only when running the app without IIS.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1065">如需 ASP.NET Core 模組組態指南，請參閱 <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1065">For ASP.NET Core Module configuration guidance, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1066">如需代管的詳細資訊，請參閱[在 ASP.NET Core 中代管](xref:fundamentals/index#host)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1066">For more information on hosting, see [Host in ASP.NET Core](xref:fundamentals/index#host).</span></span>

## <a name="application-configuration"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1067">應用程式設定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1067">Application configuration</span></span>

### <a name="enable-the-iisintegration-components"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1068">啟用 IISIntegration 元件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1068">Enable the IISIntegration components</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1069">在 `CreateWebHostBuilder` (*Program.cs*) 中建立主機時，請呼叫 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.WebHost.CreateDefaultBuilder*> 以啟用 IIS 整合：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1069">When building a host in `CreateWebHostBuilder` (*Program.cs*), call <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.WebHost.CreateDefaultBuilder*> to enable IIS integration:</span></span>

```csharp
public static IWebHostBuilder CreateWebHostBuilder(string[] args) =>
    WebHost.CreateDefaultBuilder(args)
        ...
```

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1070">如需 `CreateDefaultBuilder` 的詳細資訊，請參閱 <xref:fundamentals/host/web-host#set-up-a-host>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1070">For more information on `CreateDefaultBuilder`, see <xref:fundamentals/host/web-host#set-up-a-host>.</span></span>

### <a name="iis-options"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1071">IIS 選項</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1071">IIS options</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1072">選項</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1072">Option</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1073">預設</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1073">Default</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1074">設定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1074">Setting</span></span> |
| ------------------------------ | :-----: | ------- |
| `AutomaticAuthentication`      | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1075">若為 `true`，IIS 伺服器會設定由 [Windows 驗證](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth)所驗證的 `HttpContext.User`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1075">If `true`, IIS Server sets the `HttpContext.User` authenticated by [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1076">若為 `false`，則伺服器僅會對 `HttpContext.User` 提供身分識別，並在 `AuthenticationScheme` 明確要求時回應挑戰。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1076">If `false`, the server only provides an identity for `HttpContext.User` and responds to challenges when explicitly requested by the `AuthenticationScheme`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1077">必須在 IIS 中啟用 Windows 驗證以讓 `AutomaticAuthentication` 作用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1077">Windows Authentication must be enabled in IIS for `AutomaticAuthentication` to function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1078">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [Windows 驗證](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1078">For more information, see [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> |
| `AuthenticationDisplayName`    | `null`  | <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1079">設定使用者在登入頁面上看到的顯示名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1079">Sets the display name shown to users on login pages.</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1080">若要設定 IIS 選項，請在 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*> 中加入 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISOptions> 的服務設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1080">To configure IIS options, include a service configuration for <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISOptions> in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1081">下列範例會防止應用程式填入 `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate`：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1081">The following example prevents the app from populating `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.Configure<IISOptions>(options => 
{
    options.ForwardClientCertificate = false;
});
```

| <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1082">選項</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1082">Option</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1083">預設</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1083">Default</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1084">設定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1084">Setting</span></span> |
| ------------------------------ | :-----: | ------- |
| `AutomaticAuthentication`      | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1085">若為 `true`，[IIS 整合中介軟體](#enable-the-iisintegration-components)會設定由 [Windows 驗證](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth)所驗證的 `HttpContext.User`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1085">If `true`, [IIS Integration Middleware](#enable-the-iisintegration-components) sets the `HttpContext.User` authenticated by [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1086">如果為 `false`，則驗證中介軟體僅針對 `HttpContext.User` 提供身分識別，並在游 `AuthenticationScheme` 提出明確要求時回應挑戰。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1086">If `false`, the middleware only provides an identity for `HttpContext.User` and responds to challenges when explicitly requested by the `AuthenticationScheme`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1087">必須在 IIS 中啟用 Windows 驗證以讓 `AutomaticAuthentication` 作用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1087">Windows Authentication must be enabled in IIS for `AutomaticAuthentication` to function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1088">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [Windows 驗證](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth)主題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1088">For more information, see the [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth) topic.</span></span> |
| `AuthenticationDisplayName`    | `null`  | <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1089">設定使用者在登入頁面上看到的顯示名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1089">Sets the display name shown to users on login pages.</span></span> |
| `ForwardClientCertificate`     | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1090">如果為 `true` 且 `MS-ASPNETCORE-CLIENTCERT` 要求標頭已存在，則會填入 `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1090">If `true` and the `MS-ASPNETCORE-CLIENTCERT` request header is present, the `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate` is populated.</span></span> |

### <a name="proxy-server-and-load-balancer-scenarios"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1091">Proxy 伺服器和負載平衡器案例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1091">Proxy server and load balancer scenarios</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1092">用來設定轉送標頭中介軟體及 ASP.NET Core 模組的 [IIS 整合中介軟體](#enable-the-iisintegration-components)會設定為轉送配置 (HTTP/HTTPS) 與發出要求的遠端 IP 位址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1092">The [IIS Integration Middleware](#enable-the-iisintegration-components), which configures Forwarded Headers Middleware, and the ASP.NET Core Module are configured to forward the scheme (HTTP/HTTPS) and the remote IP address where the request originated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1093">其他 Proxy 伺服器和負載平衡器後方託管的應用程式可能需要其他設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1093">Additional configuration might be required for apps hosted behind additional proxy servers and load balancers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1094">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[設定 ASP.NET Core 以處理 Proxy 伺服器和負載平衡器](xref:host-and-deploy/proxy-load-balancer)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1094">For more information, see [Configure ASP.NET Core to work with proxy servers and load balancers](xref:host-and-deploy/proxy-load-balancer).</span></span>

### <a name="webconfig-file"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1095">web.config 檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1095">web.config file</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1096">*web.config* 檔案是用來設定 [ASP.NET Core 模組](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1096">The *web.config* file configures the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1097">發佈專案時，由 MSBuild 目標 (`_TransformWebConfig`) 處理 *web.config* 檔案的建立、轉換及發佈。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1097">Creating, transforming, and publishing the *web.config* file is handled by an MSBuild target (`_TransformWebConfig`) when the project is published.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1098">此目標存在於 Web SDK 目標 (`Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1098">This target is present in the Web SDK targets (`Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1099">SDK 設定在專案檔的頂端：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1099">The SDK is set at the top of the project file:</span></span>

```xml
<Project Sdk="Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web">
```

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1100">如果專案中沒有 *web.config* 檔案，則系統會使用正確的 *processPath* 和 *arguments* 建立該檔案以設定 ASP.NET Core 模組，並將該檔案移至[已發行的輸出](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1100">If a *web.config* file isn't present in the project, the file is created with the correct *processPath* and *arguments* to configure the ASP.NET Core Module and moved to [published output](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1101">如果 *web.config* 檔案存在於專案中，則系統會使用正確的 *processPath* 和 *arguments* 來轉換該檔案以設定 ASP.NET Core 模組，然後將它移至已發行的輸出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1101">If a *web.config* file is present in the project, the file is transformed with the correct *processPath* and *arguments* to configure the ASP.NET Core Module and moved to published output.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1102">轉換不會修改檔案中的 IIS 組態設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1102">The transformation doesn't modify IIS configuration settings in the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1103">*web.config* 檔案可提供能控制作用中 IIS 模組的額外 IIS 組態設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1103">The *web.config* file may provide additional IIS configuration settings that control active IIS modules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1104">如需能處理 ASP.NET Core 應用程式要求之 IIS 模組的相關資訊，請參閱 [IIS 模組](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules)主題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1104">For information on IIS modules that are capable of processing requests with ASP.NET Core apps, see the [IIS modules](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules) topic.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1105">若要防止 Web SDK 轉換*web.config*檔案，請使用專案檔 **\<IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>** 中的屬性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1105">To prevent the Web SDK from transforming the *web.config* file, use the **\<IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>** property in the project file:</span></span>

```xml
<PropertyGroup>
  <IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>true</IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>
</PropertyGroup>
```

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1106">使 Web SDK 無法轉換檔案時，應該由開發人員手動設定 *processPath* 和 *arguments*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1106">When disabling the Web SDK from transforming the file, the *processPath* and *arguments* should be manually set by the developer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1107">如需詳細資訊，請參閱<xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1107">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

### <a name="webconfig-file-location"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1108">web.config 檔案位置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1108">web.config file location</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1109">為了正確設定[ASP.NET Core 模組](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module)， *web.config*檔案必須存在於[內容根](xref:fundamentals/index#content-root)路徑 (通常是已部署應用程式的應用程式基底路徑) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1109">In order to set up the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) correctly, the *web.config* file must be present at the [content root](xref:fundamentals/index#content-root) path (typically the app base path) of the deployed app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1110">這是與提供給 IIS 的網站實體路徑相同的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1110">This is the same location as the website physical path provided to IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1111">應用程式的根目錄需有 *web.config* 檔案，才能使用 Web Deploy 發行多個應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1111">The *web.config* file is required at the root of the app to enable the publishing of multiple apps using Web Deploy.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1112">機密檔案存在於應用程式的實體路徑上，例如\* \<assembly>.runtimeconfig.json*、 \* \<assembly> .xml* (xml 檔批註) ，以及\* \<assembly> 上的.deps.js\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1112">Sensitive files exist on the app's physical path, such as *\<assembly>.runtimeconfig.json*, *\<assembly>.xml* (XML Documentation comments), and *\<assembly>.deps.json*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1113">當 *web.config* 檔案存在且網站正常啟動時，如果有人要求機密檔案，IIS 不會予以提供。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1113">When the *web.config* file is present and the site starts normally, IIS doesn't serve these sensitive files if they're requested.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1114">若 *web.config* 檔案遺失或沒有正確命名，或是無法設定網站以正常啟動，IIS 可能會公開提供機密檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1114">If the *web.config* file is missing, incorrectly named, or unable to configure the site for normal startup, IIS may serve sensitive files publicly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1115">\***web.config*檔案必須隨時存在於部署中、正確命名，而且能夠將網站設定為正常啟動。絕對不要從生產環境部署移除*web.config\*檔案。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1115">**The *web.config* file must be present in the deployment at all times, correctly named, and able to configure the site for normal start up. Never remove the *web.config* file from a production deployment.**</span></span>

### <a name="transform-webconfig"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1116">轉換 web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1116">Transform web.config</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1117">如需在發佈時轉換 *web.config* (例如依據設定、設定檔或環境設定環境變數)，請參閱<xref:host-and-deploy/iis/transform-webconfig>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1117">If you need to transform *web.config* on publish (for example, set environment variables based on the configuration, profile, or environment), see <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/transform-webconfig>.</span></span>

## <a name="iis-configuration"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1118">IIS 組態</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1118">IIS configuration</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1119">**Windows Server 作業系統**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1119">**Windows Server operating systems**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1120">啟用**網頁伺服器 (IIS)** 伺服器角色，並建立角色服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1120">Enable the **Web Server (IIS)** server role and establish role services.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1121">使用來自 [管理]\*\*\*\* 功能表的 [新增角色及功能]\*\*\*\* 精靈，或是 [伺服器管理員]\*\*\*\* 中的連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1121">Use the **Add Roles and Features** wizard from the **Manage** menu or the link in **Server Manager**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1122">在**伺服器角色**步驟中，核取 [網頁伺服器 (IIS)]\*\*\*\* 方塊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1122">On the **Server Roles** step, check the box for **Web Server (IIS)**.</span></span>

   ![在選取伺服器角色步驟中選取網頁伺服器 IIS 角色。](index/_static/server-roles-ws2016.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1124">在 [功能]\*\*\*\* 步驟之後，[角色服務]\*\*\*\* 步驟會針對網頁伺服器 (IIS) 進行載入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1124">After the **Features** step, the **Role services** step loads for Web Server (IIS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1125">選取所需的 IIS 角色服務或接受所提供的預設角色服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1125">Select the IIS role services desired or accept the default role services provided.</span></span>

   ![在選取角色服務步驟中，選取預設的角色服務。](index/_static/role-services-ws2016.png)

   <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1127">**Windows 驗證 (選擇性)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1127">**Windows Authentication (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1128">若要啟用 Windows 驗證，請展開下列節點： [**網頁伺服器**  >  **安全性**]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1128">To enable Windows Authentication, expand the following nodes: **Web Server** > **Security**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1129">選取 [Windows 驗證]\*\*\*\* 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1129">Select the **Windows Authentication** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1130">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[Windows 驗證 \<windowsAuthentication> ](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/)和[設定 windows 驗證](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1130">For more information, see [Windows Authentication \<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) and [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1131">**WebSocket (選擇性)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1131">**WebSockets (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1132">WebSocket 由 ASP.NET Core 1.1 或更新版本所支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1132">WebSockets is supported with ASP.NET Core 1.1 or later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1133">若要啟用 websocket，請展開下列節點： [**網頁伺服器**  >  **應用程式開發**]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1133">To enable WebSockets, expand the following nodes: **Web Server** > **Application Development**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1134">選取 [WebSocket 通訊協定]\*\*\*\* 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1134">Select the **WebSocket Protocol** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1135">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1135">For more information, see [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1136">透過**確認**步驟繼續作業，安裝網頁伺服器角色和服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1136">Proceed through the **Confirmation** step to install the web server role and services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1137">安裝\*\*Web 服務器 (iis) \*\*角色之後，不需要重新開機伺服器/iis。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1137">A server/IIS restart isn't required after installing the **Web Server (IIS)** role.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1138">**Windows 桌面作業系統**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1138">**Windows desktop operating systems**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1139">啟用 [IIS 管理主控台]\*\*\*\* 和 [World Wide Web 服務]\*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1139">Enable the **IIS Management Console** and **World Wide Web Services**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1140">瀏覽到 [控制台]\*\* [程式]\*\* > \*\* [程式和功能]\*\* > \*\*\*\* > **[開啟或關閉 Windows 功能]** \(畫面左側\)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1140">Navigate to **Control Panel** > **Programs** > **Programs and Features** > **Turn Windows features on or off** (left side of the screen).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1141">開啟 [Internet Information Services]\*\*\*\* 節點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1141">Open the **Internet Information Services** node.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1142">開啟 [Web 管理工具]\*\*\*\* 節點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1142">Open the **Web Management Tools** node.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1143">核取 [IIS 管理主控台]\*\*\*\* 方塊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1143">Check the box for **IIS Management Console**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1144">[World Wide Web Services] (全球資訊網服務)\*\*\*\* 核取方塊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1144">Check the box for **World Wide Web Services**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1145">接受**全球資訊網服務**的預設功能，或自訂 IIS 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1145">Accept the default features for **World Wide Web Services** or customize the IIS features.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1146">**Windows 驗證 (選擇性)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1146">**Windows Authentication (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1147">若要啟用 Windows 驗證，請展開下列節點： **World Wide Web 服務**  >  **安全性**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1147">To enable Windows Authentication, expand the following nodes: **World Wide Web Services** > **Security**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1148">選取 [Windows 驗證]\*\*\*\* 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1148">Select the **Windows Authentication** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1149">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[Windows 驗證 \<windowsAuthentication> ](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/)和[設定 windows 驗證](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1149">For more information, see [Windows Authentication \<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) and [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1150">**WebSocket (選擇性)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1150">**WebSockets (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1151">WebSocket 由 ASP.NET Core 1.1 或更新版本所支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1151">WebSockets is supported with ASP.NET Core 1.1 or later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1152">若要啟用 websocket，請展開下列節點： [ **World Wide Web 服務**] [  >  **應用程式開發] 功能**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1152">To enable WebSockets, expand the following nodes: **World Wide Web Services** > **Application Development Features**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1153">選取 [WebSocket 通訊協定]\*\*\*\* 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1153">Select the **WebSocket Protocol** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1154">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1154">For more information, see [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1155">若 IIS 安裝需要重新啟動，請重新啟動系統。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1155">If the IIS installation requires a restart, restart the system.</span></span>

![選取 [Windows 功能] 中的 [IIS 管理主控台] 和 [World Wide Web Services] (全球資訊網服務)。](index/_static/windows-features-win10.png)

## <a name="install-the-net-core-hosting-bundle"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1157">安裝 .NET Core 裝載套件組合</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1157">Install the .NET Core Hosting Bundle</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1158">在主控系統上安裝 .NET Core 裝載套件組合\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1158">Install the *.NET Core Hosting Bundle* on the hosting system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1159">套件組合會安裝 .NET Core 執行時間、.NET Core 程式庫和[ASP.NET Core 模組](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1159">The bundle installs the .NET Core Runtime, .NET Core Library, and the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1160">此模組可讓 ASP.NET Core 應用程式在 IIS 背後執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1160">The module allows ASP.NET Core apps to run behind IIS.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1161">若裝載套件組合在 IIS 之前安裝，則必須對該套件組合安裝進行修復。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1161">If the Hosting Bundle is installed before IIS, the bundle installation must be repaired.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1162">請在安裝 IIS 之後，再次執行裝載套件組合安裝程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1162">Run the Hosting Bundle installer again after installing IIS.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1163">如果在安裝 64 位元 (x64) 版本的 .NET Core 後才安裝裝載套件組合，那麼可能會遺漏 SDK ([未偵測到 .NET Core SDK](xref:test/troubleshoot#no-net-core-sdks-were-detected))。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1163">If the Hosting Bundle is installed after installing the 64-bit (x64) version of .NET Core, SDKs might appear to be missing ([No .NET Core SDKs were detected](xref:test/troubleshoot#no-net-core-sdks-were-detected)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1164">若要解決此問題，請參閱 <xref:test/troubleshoot#missing-sdk-after-installing-the-net-core-hosting-bundle>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1164">To resolve the problem, see <xref:test/troubleshoot#missing-sdk-after-installing-the-net-core-hosting-bundle>.</span></span>

### <a name="download"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1165">下載</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1165">Download</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1166">流覽至 [[下載 .Net Core](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/download/dotnet-core) ] 頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1166">Navigate to the [Download .NET Core](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/download/dotnet-core) page.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1167">選取所需的 .NET Core 版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1167">Select the desired .NET Core version.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1168">在 [執行應用程式 - 執行階段]\*\*\*\* 欄中，尋找想要的 .NET Core 執行階段版本列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1168">In the **Run apps - Runtime** column, find the row of the .NET Core runtime version desired.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1169">使用**裝載**套件組合連結來下載安裝程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1169">Download the installer using the **Hosting Bundle** link.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1170">某些安裝程式包含已達到期生命週期結束 (EOL) 的發行版本，這些發行版本已不受 Microsoft 支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1170">Some installers contain release versions that have reached their end of life (EOL) and are no longer supported by Microsoft.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1171">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[支援原則](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/platform/support/policy/dotnet-core) \(英文 \)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1171">For more information, see the [support policy](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/platform/support/policy/dotnet-core).</span></span>

### <a name="install-the-hosting-bundle"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1172">安裝裝載套件組合</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1172">Install the Hosting Bundle</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1173">在伺服器上執行安裝程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1173">Run the installer on the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1174">從系統管理員命令殼層執行安裝程式時，有 下列參數可用：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1174">The following parameters are available when running the installer from an administrator command shell:</span></span>

   * <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1175">`OPT_NO_ANCM=1`：略過安裝 ASP.NET Core 模組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1175">`OPT_NO_ANCM=1`: Skip installing the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1176">`OPT_NO_RUNTIME=1`：略過安裝 .NET Core 執行時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1176">`OPT_NO_RUNTIME=1`: Skip installing the .NET Core runtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1177">當伺服器僅裝載[獨立部署 (SCD) ](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd)時使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1177">Used when the server only hosts [self-contained deployments (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1178">`OPT_NO_SHAREDFX=1`：略過安裝 ASP.NET 共用架構 (ASP.NET 執行時間) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1178">`OPT_NO_SHAREDFX=1`: Skip installing the ASP.NET Shared Framework (ASP.NET runtime).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1179">當伺服器僅裝載[獨立部署 (SCD) ](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd)時使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1179">Used when the server only hosts [self-contained deployments (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1180">`OPT_NO_X86=1`：略過安裝 x86 執行時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1180">`OPT_NO_X86=1`: Skip installing x86 runtimes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1181">當您確定不會裝載 32 位元應用程式時，請使用此參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1181">Use this parameter when you know that you won't be hosting 32-bit apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1182">如果將來有可能同時裝載 32 位元和 64 位元應用程式，請不要使用此參數並安裝這兩個執行階段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1182">If there's any chance that you will host both 32-bit and 64-bit apps in the future, don't use this parameter and install both runtimes.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1183">`OPT_NO_SHARED_CONFIG_CHECK=1`：當共用設定 (*applicationHost.config*) 位於與 iis 安裝相同的電腦上時，停用 [檢查使用 IIS 共用設定]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1183">`OPT_NO_SHARED_CONFIG_CHECK=1`: Disable the check for using an IIS Shared Configuration when the shared configuration (*applicationHost.config*) is on the same machine as the IIS installation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1184">*只在 ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更新版本的裝載套件組合安裝程式上可用。*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1184">*Only available for ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later Hosting Bundler installers.*</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1185">如需詳細資訊，請參閱<xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1185">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration>.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1186">重新開機系統，或在命令 shell 中執行下列命令：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1186">Restart the system or execute the following commands in a command shell:</span></span>

   ```console
   net stop was /y
   net start w3svc
   ```
   <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1187">重新啟動 IIS 將能偵測到由安裝程式對系統路徑 (此為環境變數) 所做出的變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1187">Restarting IIS picks up a change to the system PATH, which is an environment variable, made by the installer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1188">安裝裝載套件組合時，不需要手動停止 IIS 中的個別網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1188">It isn't necessary to manually stop individual sites in IIS when installing the Hosting Bundle.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1189">在 IIS 重新開機時，) 重新開機 (IIS 網站的託管應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1189">Hosted apps (IIS sites) restart when IIS restarts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1190">應用程式會在收到第一個要求時重新開機，包括從[應用程式初始化模組](#application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1190">Apps start up again when they receive their first request, including from the [Application Initialization Module](#application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1191">ASP.NET Core 採用共用架構封裝修補程式版本的向前復原行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1191">ASP.NET Core adopts roll-forward behavior for patch releases of shared framework packages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1192">當 IIS 所裝載的應用程式使用 IIS 重新開機時，應用程式會在收到第一個要求時，以其所參考套件的最新修補程式版本來載入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1192">When apps hosted by IIS restart with IIS, the apps load with the latest patch releases of their referenced packages when they receive their first request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1193">如果未重新開機 IIS，應用程式會在其工作者進程回收時重新開機並展示向前復原行為，並接收其第一個要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1193">If IIS isn't restarted, apps restart and exhibit roll-forward behavior when their worker processes are recycled and they receive their first request.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1194">如需 IIS 共用組態的資訊，請參閱[使用 IIS 共用組態的 ASP.NET Core 模組](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1194">For information on IIS Shared Configuration, see [ASP.NET Core Module with IIS Shared Configuration](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration).</span></span>

## <a name="install-web-deploy-when-publishing-with-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1195">使用 Visual Studio 發佈時安裝 Web Deploy</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1195">Install Web Deploy when publishing with Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1196">將應用程式部署到具有 [Web Deploy](/iis/install/installing-publishing-technologies/installing-and-configuring-web-deploy-on-iis-80-or-later) 的伺服器時，請在伺服器上安裝最新版的 Web Deploy。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1196">When deploying apps to servers with [Web Deploy](/iis/install/installing-publishing-technologies/installing-and-configuring-web-deploy-on-iis-80-or-later), install the latest version of Web Deploy on the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1197">若要安裝 Web Deploy，請使用 [Web Platform Installer (WebPI)](https://www.microsoft.com/web/downloads/platform.aspx) 或從 [Microsoft 下載中心](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=43717)直接取得安裝程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1197">To install Web Deploy, use the [Web Platform Installer (WebPI)](https://www.microsoft.com/web/downloads/platform.aspx) or obtain an installer directly from the [Microsoft Download Center](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=43717).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1198">慣用的方法是使用 WebPI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1198">The preferred method is to use WebPI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1199">WebPI 提供獨立的安裝程式和組態以裝載提供者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1199">WebPI offers a standalone setup and a configuration for hosting providers.</span></span>

## <a name="create-the-iis-site"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1200">建立 IIS 網站</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1200">Create the IIS site</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1201">在主控系統上，請建立資料夾以容納應用程式的已發行資料夾和檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1201">On the hosting system, create a folder to contain the app's published folders and files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1202">在下列步驟中，您提供資料夾路徑給 IIS，作為應用程式的實體路徑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1202">In a following step, the folder's path is provided to IIS as the physical path to the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1203">如需應用程式之部署資料夾和檔案配置的詳細資訊，請參閱 <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1203">For more information on an app's deployment folder and file layout, see <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1204">在 [IIS 管理員] 中 **，在 [** 連線] 面板中開啟伺服器的節點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1204">In IIS Manager, open the server's node in the **Connections** panel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1205">以滑鼠右鍵按一下 [網站]\*\*\*\* 資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1205">Right-click the **Sites** folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1206">從操作功能表選取 [新增網站]\*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1206">Select **Add Website** from the contextual menu.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1207">提供**網站名稱**，並將**實體路徑**設定為應用程式的部署資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1207">Provide a **Site name** and set the **Physical path** to the app's deployment folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1208">藉由**Binding**選取 **[確定]** 來提供系結設定並建立網站：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1208">Provide the **Binding** configuration and create the website by selecting **OK**:</span></span>

   ![在新增網站步驟中提供站台名稱、實體路徑和主機名稱。](index/_static/add-website-ws2016.png)

   > [!WARNING]
   > <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1210">請**勿**使用最上層萬用字元繫結 (`http://*:80/`與 `http://+:80`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1210">Top-level wildcard bindings (`http://*:80/` and `http://+:80`) should **not** be used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1211">最上層萬用字元繫結可能暴露您的應用程式安全性弱點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1211">Top-level wildcard bindings can open up your app to security vulnerabilities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1212">這對強式與弱式萬用字元皆適用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1212">This applies to both strong and weak wildcards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1213">請使用明確主機名稱，而非萬用字元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1213">Use explicit host names rather than wildcards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1214">若您擁有整個父網域 (與具弱點的 `*.com` 相對) 的控制權，則子網域萬用字元繫結 (例如 `*.mysub.com`) 就沒有此安全性風險。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1214">Subdomain wildcard binding (for example, `*.mysub.com`) doesn't have this security risk if you control the entire parent domain (as opposed to `*.com`, which is vulnerable).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1215">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [rfc7230 5.4 節](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7230#section-5.4)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1215">See [rfc7230 section-5.4](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7230#section-5.4) for more information.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1216">在伺服器的節點之下，選取 [應用程式集區]\*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1216">Under the server's node, select **Application Pools**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1217">以滑鼠右鍵按一下網站的應用程式集區，然後從操作功能表選取 [基本設定]\*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1217">Right-click the site's app pool and select **Basic Settings** from the contextual menu.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1218">在 [編輯應用程式集區]\*\*\*\* 視窗中，將 [.NET CLR 版本]\*\*\*\* 設定為 [沒有受控碼]\*\*\*\*：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1218">In the **Edit Application Pool** window, set the **.NET CLR version** to **No Managed Code**:</span></span>

   ![將 .NET CLR 版本設為 [沒有受控碼]。](index/_static/edit-apppool-ws2016.png)

    <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1220">ASP.NET Core 會在不同的處理序中執行，並管理執行階段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1220">ASP.NET Core runs in a separate process and manages the runtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1221">ASP.NET Core 不仰賴載入桌面 CLR (.NET CLR)&mdash;會使用 .NET Core 的核心通用語言執行平台 (CoreCLR) 來開機以在背景工作處理序中裝載應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1221">ASP.NET Core doesn't rely on loading the desktop CLR (.NET CLR)&mdash;the Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) for .NET Core is booted to host the app in the worker process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1222">將 [.NET CLR 版本]\*\*\*\* 設定為 [沒有受控碼]\*\*\*\* 是選擇性的，但建議這樣做。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1222">Setting the **.NET CLR version** to **No Managed Code** is optional but recommended.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1223">*ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更新版本*：對於使用[同處理序主控模型](#in-process-hosting-model)的 64 位元 (x64) [獨立式部署](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd)，會停用 32 位元 (x86) 處理序的應用程式集區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1223">*ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later*: For a 64-bit (x64) [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) that uses the [in-process hosting model](#in-process-hosting-model), disable the app pool for 32-bit (x86) processes.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1224">在 IIS 管理員的 [動作]\*\*\*\* 資訊看板 > [應用程式集區]\*\*\*\* 中，選取 [設定應用程式集區預設值]\*\*\*\* 或 [進階設定]\*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1224">In the **Actions** sidebar of IIS Manager > **Application Pools**, select **Set Application Pool Defaults** or **Advanced Settings**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1225">找到 [啟用 32 位元應用程式]\*\*\*\*，然後將其值設定為 `False`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1225">Locate **Enable 32-Bit Applications** and set the value to `False`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1226">此設定不會影響為[處理程序外裝載](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#out-of-process-hosting-model)部署的應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1226">This setting doesn't affect apps deployed for [out-of-process hosting](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#out-of-process-hosting-model).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1227">確認處理序模型身分識別具有適當的權限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1227">Confirm the process model identity has the proper permissions.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1228">如果應用程式集區的預設識別 (**進程模型**  >  **Identity**) 從\*\* Identity ApplicationPool\*\*變更為另一個身分識別，請確認新的身分識別具有存取應用程式資料夾、資料庫和其他必要資源的必要許可權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1228">If the default identity of the app pool (**Process Model** > **Identity**) is changed from **ApplicationPoolIdentity** to another identity, verify that the new identity has the required permissions to access the app's folder, database, and other required resources.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1229">例如，應用程式集區需要針對應用程式讀取和寫入檔案的資料夾取得讀取和寫入權限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1229">For example, the app pool requires read and write access to folders where the app reads and writes files.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1230">**Windows 驗證設定 (選擇性)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1230">**Windows Authentication configuration (Optional)**</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1231">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[設定 Windows 驗證](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth)主題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1231">For more information, see [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

## <a name="deploy-the-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1232">部署應用程式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1232">Deploy the app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1233">將應用程式部署至在[建立 IIS 網站](#create-the-iis-site)一節中所建立的 IIS **實體路徑**資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1233">Deploy the app to the IIS **Physical path** folder that was established in the [Create the IIS site](#create-the-iis-site) section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1234">[Web Deploy](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) 是建議的部署機制，但有數個選項可將應用程式從專案的 [publish]\*\* 資料夾移動至主機系統的部署資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1234">[Web Deploy](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) is the recommended mechanism for deployment, but several options exist for moving the app from the project's *publish* folder to the hosting system's deployment folder.</span></span>

### <a name="web-deploy-with-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1235">使用 Visual Studio 的 Web Deploy</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1235">Web Deploy with Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1236">請參閱[適用於 ASP.NET Core 應用程式部署的 Visual Studio 發行設定檔](xref:host-and-deploy/visual-studio-publish-profiles#publish-profiles)主題，了解如何建立搭配 Web Deploy 使用的發行設定檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1236">See the [Visual Studio publish profiles for ASP.NET Core app deployment](xref:host-and-deploy/visual-studio-publish-profiles#publish-profiles) topic to learn how to create a publish profile for use with Web Deploy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1237">如果主機服務提供者提供或支援建立發行設定檔，請下載其設定檔，並使用 Visual Studio 的 [發行]\*\*\*\* 對話方塊匯入其設定檔：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1237">If the hosting provider provides a Publish Profile or support for creating one, download their profile and import it using the Visual Studio **Publish** dialog:</span></span>

![[發佈] 對話方塊頁](index/_static/pub-dialog.png)

### <a name="web-deploy-outside-of-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1239">Visual Studio 外部的 Web Deploy</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1239">Web Deploy outside of Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1240">透過命令列也可以在 Visual Studio 外部使用 [Web Deploy](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1240">[Web Deploy](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) can also be used outside of Visual Studio from the command line.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1241">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [Web 部署工具](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/use-the-web-deployment-tool)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1241">For more information, see [Web Deployment Tool](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/use-the-web-deployment-tool).</span></span>

### <a name="alternatives-to-web-deploy"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1242">Web Deploy 的替代項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1242">Alternatives to Web Deploy</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1243">使用數種方法的其中一種將應用程式移到主機系統，例如手動複製、[Xcopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/xcopy)、[Robocopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/robocopy) 或 [PowerShell](/powershell/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1243">Use any of several methods to move the app to the hosting system, such as manual copy, [Xcopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/xcopy), [Robocopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/robocopy), or [PowerShell](/powershell/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1244">如需 IIS 的 ASP.NET Core 部署詳細資訊，請參閱 [IIS 系統管理員的部署資源](#deployment-resources-for-iis-administrators)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1244">For more information on ASP.NET Core deployment to IIS, see the [Deployment resources for IIS administrators](#deployment-resources-for-iis-administrators) section.</span></span>

## <a name="browse-the-website"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1245">瀏覽網站</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1245">Browse the website</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1246">應用程式部署到主機系統之後，請向其中一個應用程式的公用端點發出要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1246">After the app is deployed to the hosting system, make a request to one of the app's public endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1247">在下列範例中，網站繫結至 IIS 上的**連接埠** `80`，其**主機名稱**為 `www.mysite.com`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1247">In the following example, the site is bound to an IIS **Host name** of `www.mysite.com` on **Port** `80`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f8aa-1248">對 `http://www.mysite.com` 發出要求：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f8aa-1248">A request is made to `http://www.mysite.com`:</span></span>
